Pali: 2.5.1. Akusalacitta 

vb6:49.1
Pali: Katame dhammā akusalā? 

vb6:49.2
Pali: Yasmiṁ samaye akusalaṁ cittaṁ uppannaṁ hoti somanassasahagataṁ diṭṭhigatasampayuttaṁ rūpārammaṇaṁ vā saddārammaṇaṁ vā gandhārammaṇaṁ vā rasārammaṇaṁ vā phoṭṭhabbārammaṇaṁ vā dhammārammaṇaṁ vā yaṁ yaṁ vā panārabbha, tasmiṁ samaye avijjāpaccayā saṅkhāro, saṅkhārapaccayā viññāṇaṁ, viññāṇapaccayā nāmaṁ, nāmapaccayā chaṭṭhāyatanaṁ, chaṭṭhāyatanapaccayā phasso, phassapaccayā vedanā, vedanāpaccayā taṇhā, taṇhāpaccayā upādānaṁ, upādānapaccayā bhavo, bhavapaccayā jāti, jātipaccayā jarāmaraṇaṁ. 

vb6:49.3
Pali: Evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa samudayo hoti. 

vb6:50.1
Pali: Tattha katamā avijjā? 

vb6:50.2
Pali: Yaṁ aññāṇaṁ adassanaṁ …pe… avijjālaṅgī moho akusalamūlaṁ—

vb6:50.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “avijjā”. 

vb6:51.1
Pali: Tattha katamo avijjāpaccayā saṅkhāro? 

vb6:51.2
Pali: Yā cetanā sañcetanā sañcetayitattaṁ—

vb6:51.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “avijjāpaccayā saṅkhāro”. 

vb6:52.1
Pali: Tattha katamaṁ saṅkhārapaccayā viññāṇaṁ? 

vb6:52.2
Pali: Yaṁ cittaṁ mano mānasaṁ hadayaṁ paṇḍaraṁ mano manāyatanaṁ manindriyaṁ viññāṇaṁ viññāṇakkhandho tajjāmanoviññāṇadhātu—

vb6:52.3
Pali: idaṁ vuccati “saṅkhārapaccayā viññāṇaṁ”. 

vb6:53.1
Pali: Tattha katamaṁ viññāṇapaccayā nāmaṁ? 

vb6:53.2
Pali: Vedanākkhandho, saññākkhandho, saṅkhārakkhandho—

vb6:53.3
Pali: idaṁ vuccati “viññāṇapaccayā nāmaṁ”. 

vb6:54.1
Pali: Tattha katamaṁ nāmapaccayā chaṭṭhāyatanaṁ? 

vb6:54.2
Pali: Yaṁ cittaṁ mano mānasaṁ hadayaṁ paṇḍaraṁ mano manāyatanaṁ manindriyaṁ viññāṇaṁ viññāṇakkhandho tajjāmanoviññāṇadhātu—

vb6:54.3
Pali: idaṁ vuccati “nāmapaccayā chaṭṭhāyatanaṁ”. 

vb6:55.1
Pali: Tattha katamo chaṭṭhāyatanapaccayā phasso? 

vb6:55.2
Pali: Yo phasso phusanā samphusanā samphusitattaṁ—

vb6:55.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “chaṭṭhāyatanapaccayā phasso”. 

vb6:56.1
Pali: Tattha katamā phassapaccayā vedanā? 

vb6:56.2
Pali: Yaṁ cetasikaṁ sātaṁ cetasikaṁ sukhaṁ cetosamphassajaṁ sātaṁ sukhaṁ vedayitaṁ cetosamphassajā sātā sukhā vedanā—

vb6:56.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “phassapaccayā vedanā”. 

vb6:57.1
Pali: Tattha katamā vedanāpaccayā taṇhā? 

vb6:57.2
Pali: Yo rāgo sārāgo anunayo anurodho nandī nandirāgo cittassa sārāgo—

vb6:57.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “vedanāpaccayā taṇhā”. 

vb6:58.1
Pali: Tattha katamaṁ taṇhāpaccayā upādānaṁ? 

vb6:58.2
Pali: Yā diṭṭhi diṭṭhigataṁ diṭṭhigahanaṁ diṭṭhikantāro diṭṭhivisūkāyikaṁ diṭṭhivipphanditaṁ diṭṭhisaṁyojanaṁ gāho patiṭṭhāho abhiniveso parāmāso kummaggo micchāpatho micchattaṁ titthāyatanaṁ vipariyāsaggāho—

vb6:58.3
Pali: idaṁ vuccati “taṇhāpaccayā upādānaṁ”. 

vb6:59.1
Pali: Tattha katamo upādānapaccayā bhavo? 

vb6:59.2
Pali: Ṭhapetvā upādānaṁ, vedanākkhandho saññākkhandho saṅkhārakkhandho viññāṇakkhandho—

vb6:59.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “upādānapaccayā bhavo”. 

vb6:60.1
Pali: Tattha katamā bhavapaccayā jāti? 

vb6:60.2
Pali: Yā tesaṁ tesaṁ dhammānaṁ jāti sañjāti nibbatti abhinibbatti pātubhāvo—

vb6:60.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “bhavapaccayā jāti”. 

vb6:61.1
Pali: Tattha katamaṁ jātipaccayā jarāmaraṇaṁ? 

vb6:61.2
Pali: Atthi jarā, atthi maraṇaṁ. 

vb6:61.3
Pali: Tattha katamā jarā? 

vb6:61.4
Pali: Yā tesaṁ tesaṁ dhammānaṁ jarā jīraṇatā āyuno saṁhāni—

vb6:61.5
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “jarā”. 

vb6:61.6
Pali: Tattha katamaṁ maraṇaṁ? 

vb6:61.7
Pali: Yo tesaṁ tesaṁ dhammānaṁ khayo vayo bhedo paribhedo aniccatā antaradhānaṁ—

vb6:61.8
Pali: idaṁ vuccati “maraṇaṁ”. 

vb6:61.9
Pali: Iti ayañca jarā, idañca maraṇaṁ. 

vb6:61.10
Pali: Idaṁ vuccati “jātipaccayā jarāmaraṇaṁ”. 

vb6:62.1

vb6:87.0
Pali: 2.6. Hetucatukka 

vb6:87.1
Pali: Tasmiṁ samaye avijjāpaccayā saṅkhāro avijjāhetuko, saṅkhārapaccayā viññāṇaṁ saṅkhārahetukaṁ, viññāṇapaccayā nāmaṁ viññāṇahetukaṁ, nāmapaccayā chaṭṭhāyatanaṁ nāmahetukaṁ, chaṭṭhāyatanapaccayā phasso chaṭṭhāyatanahetuko, phassapaccayā vedanā phassahetukā, vedanāpaccayā taṇhā vedanāhetukā, taṇhāpaccayā upādānaṁ taṇhāhetukaṁ; 

vb6:87.2
Pali: upādānapaccayā bhavo, bhavapaccayā jāti, jātipaccayā jarāmaraṇaṁ.

Pali: 2.9.  Akusalaniddesa 

vb6:221.0.2
Pali: 2.9.1 Akusalacitta 

vb6:221.1
Pali: Katame dhammā akusalā? 

vb6:221.2
Pali: Yasmiṁ samaye akusalaṁ cittaṁ uppannaṁ hoti somanassasahagataṁ diṭṭhigatasampayuttaṁ sasaṅkhārena …pe… 

vb6:221.3
Pali: somanassasahagataṁ diṭṭhigatavippayuttaṁ rūpārammaṇaṁ vā …pe… 

vb6:221.4
Pali: somanassasahagataṁ diṭṭhigatavippayuttaṁ sasaṅkhārena rūpārammaṇaṁ vā saddārammaṇaṁ vā gandhārammaṇaṁ vā rasārammaṇaṁ vā phoṭṭhabbārammaṇaṁ vā dhammārammaṇaṁ vā yaṁ yaṁ vā panārabbha, tasmiṁ samaye avijjāpaccayā saṅkhāro, saṅkhārapaccayā viññāṇaṁ, viññāṇapaccayā nāmaṁ, nāmapaccayā chaṭṭhāyatanaṁ, chaṭṭhāyatanapaccayā phasso, phassapaccayā vedanā, vedanāpaccayā taṇhā, taṇhāpaccayā adhimokkho, adhimokkhapaccayā bhavo, bhavapaccayā jāti, jātipaccayā jarāmaraṇaṁ.

Pali: Evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa samudayo hoti.

Pali: Tattha katamā avijjā?

Pali: Yaṁ cetasikaṁ asātaṁ cetasikaṁ dukkhaṁ cetosamphassajaṁ asātaṁ dukkhaṁ vedayitaṁ cetosamphassajā asātā dukkhā vedanā—

vb6:233.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “phassapaccayā vedanā”.

Pali: Tattha katamaṁ vedanāpaccayā paṭighaṁ? 

vb6:234.2

vb6:234.3
Pali: caṇḍikkaṁ asuropo anattamanatā cittassa—

vb6:234.4
Pali: idaṁ vuccati “vedanāpaccayā paṭighaṁ”. 

vb6:235.1

vb6:235.2
Pali: Yo cittassa adhimokkho adhimuccanā tadadhimuttatā—

vb6:235.3

vb6:237.0
Pali: 2.9.5. Akusalacitta 

vb6:237.1
Pali: Katame dhammā akusalā? 

vb6:237.2
Pali: Yasmiṁ samaye akusalaṁ cittaṁ uppannaṁ hoti upekkhāsahagataṁ vicikicchāsampayuttaṁ rūpārammaṇaṁ vā saddārammaṇaṁ vā gandhārammaṇaṁ vā rasārammaṇaṁ vā phoṭṭhabbārammaṇaṁ vā dhammārammaṇaṁ vā yaṁ yaṁ vā panārabbha, tasmiṁ samaye avijjāpaccayā saṅkhāro, saṅkhārapaccayā viññāṇaṁ, viññāṇapaccayā nāmaṁ, nāmapaccayā chaṭṭhāyatanaṁ, chaṭṭhāyatanapaccayā phasso, phassapaccayā vedanā, vedanāpaccayā vicikicchā, vicikicchāpaccayā bhavo, bhavapaccayā jāti, jātipaccayā jarāmaraṇaṁ. 

vb6:237.3
Pali: Evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa samudayo hoti. 

vb6:238.1
Pali: Tattha katamā avijjā? 

vb6:238.2

vb6:238.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “avijjā” …pe… 

vb6:238.4

vb6:239.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “phassapaccayā vedanā”. 

vb6:240.1
Pali: Tattha katamā vedanāpaccayā vicikicchā? 

vb6:240.2
Pali: Yā kaṅkhā kaṅkhāyanā kaṅkhāyitattaṁ vimati vicikicchā dveḷhakaṁ dvidhāpatho saṁsayo anekaṁsaggāho āsappanā parisappanā apariyogāhaṇā chambhitattaṁ cittassa manovilekho—

vb6:240.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “vedanāpaccayā vicikicchā”.

vb6:241.4

vb6:385.1

vb6:386.1
Pali: Tattha katamo chaṭṭhāyatanapaccayā phasso? 

vb6:386.2
Pali: Yo phasso phusanā samphusanā samphusitattaṁ—

vb6:386.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “chaṭṭhāyatanapaccayā phasso”. 

vb6:387.1
Pali: Tattha katamā phassapaccayā vedanā? 

vb6:387.2
Pali: Yaṁ cetasikaṁ neva sātaṁ nāsātaṁ cetosamphassajaṁ adukkhamasukhaṁ vedayitaṁ cetosamphassajā adukkhamasukhā vedanā—

vb6:387.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “phassapaccayā vedanā”. 

vb6:388.1
Pali: Tattha katamo vedanāpaccayā adhimokkho? 

vb6:388.2
Pali: Yo cittassa adhimokkho adhimuccanā tadadhimuttatā—

vb6:388.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “vedanāpaccayā adhimokkho”. 

vb6:389.1
Pali: Tattha katamo adhimokkhapaccayā bhavo? 

vb6:389.2
Pali: Ṭhapetvā adhimokkhaṁ, vedanākkhandho saññākkhandho saṅkhārakkhandho viññāṇakkhandho—

vb6:389.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “adhimokkhapaccayā bhavo”. 

vb6:390.1
Pali: Tattha katamā bhavapaccayā jāti? 

vb6:390.2
Pali: Yā tesaṁ tesaṁ dhammānaṁ jāti sañjāti nibbatti abhinibbatti pātubhāvo—

vb6:390.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “bhavapaccayā jāti”. 

vb6:391.1
Pali: Tattha katamaṁ jātipaccayā jarāmaraṇaṁ? 

vb6:391.2
Pali: Atthi jarā, atthi maraṇaṁ. 

vb6:391.3
Pali: Tattha katamā jarā? 

vb6:391.4
Pali: Yā tesaṁ tesaṁ dhammānaṁ jarā jīraṇatā āyuno saṁhāni—

vb6:391.5
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “jarā”. 

vb6:391.6
Pali: Tattha katamaṁ maraṇaṁ? 

vb6:391.7
Pali: Yo tesaṁ tesaṁ dhammānaṁ khayo vayo bhedo paribhedo aniccatā antaradhānaṁ—

vb6:391.8
Pali: idaṁ vuccati “maraṇaṁ”. 

vb6:391.9
Pali: Iti ayañca jarā, idañca maraṇaṁ. 

vb6:391.10
Pali: Idaṁ vuccati “jātipaccayā jarāmaraṇaṁ”. 

vb6:392.1
Pali: Evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa samudayo hotīti. 

vb6:392.2
Pali: Evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa saṅgati hoti, samāgamo hoti, samodhānaṁ hoti, pātubhāvo hoti. 

vb6:392.3
Pali: Tena vuccati “evametassa kevalassa dukkhakkhandhassa samudayo hotī”ti. 

vb6:393.1
Pali: Akusalamūlakavipākaniddeso. 

vb6:393.2
Pali: Abhidhammabhājanīyaṁ. 

vb6:394.1
Pali: Paṭiccasamuppādavibhaṅgo niṭṭhito.

Pali segments

vb7:0.1
Pali: Vibhaṅga 

vb7:0.2
Pali: Satipaṭṭhānavibhaṅga 

vb7:1.0
Pali: 1. Suttantabhājanīya 

vb7:1.1
Pali: Cattāro satipaṭṭhānā—

vb7:1.2
Pali: idha bhikkhu ajjhattaṁ kāye kāyānupassī viharati bahiddhā kāye kāyānupassī viharati ajjhattabahiddhā kāye kāyānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaṁ, ajjhattaṁ vedanāsu vedanānupassī viharati bahiddhā vedanāsu vedanānupassī viharati ajjhattabahiddhā vedanāsu vedanānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaṁ, ajjhattaṁ citte cittānupassī viharati bahiddhā citte cittānupassī viharati ajjhattabahiddhā citte cittānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaṁ, ajjhattaṁ dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati bahiddhā dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati ajjhattabahiddhā dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaṁ. 

vb7:2.0
Pali: 1.1. Kāyānupassanāniddesa 

vb7:2.1
Pali: Kathañca bhikkhu ajjhattaṁ kāye kāyānupassī viharati? 

vb7:2.2
Pali: Idha bhikkhu ajjhattaṁ kāyaṁ uddhaṁ pādatalā adho kesamatthakā tacapariyantaṁ pūraṁ nānappakārassa asucino paccavekkhati—

vb7:2.3
Pali: “atthi imasmiṁ kāye kesā lomā nakhā dantā taco, maṁsaṁ nhāru aṭṭhi aṭṭhimiñjaṁ vakkaṁ, hadayaṁ yakanaṁ kilomakaṁ pihakaṁ papphāsaṁ, antaṁ antaguṇaṁ udariyaṁ karīsaṁ, pittaṁ semhaṁ pubbo lohitaṁ sedo medo, assu vasā kheḷo siṅghāṇikā lasikā muttan”ti. 

vb7:2.4
Pali: So taṁ nimittaṁ āsevati bhāveti bahulīkaroti, svāvatthitaṁ vavatthapeti. 

vb7:2.5
Pali: So taṁ nimittaṁ āsevitvā bhāvetvā bahulīkaritvā svāvatthitaṁ vavatthapetvā bahiddhā kāye cittaṁ upasaṁharati. 

vb7:3.1
Pali: Kathañca bhikkhu bahiddhā kāye kāyānupassī viharati? 

vb7:3.2
Pali: Idha bhikkhu bahiddhā kāyaṁ uddhaṁ pādatalā adho kesamatthakā tacapariyantaṁ pūraṁ nānappakārassa asucino paccavekkhati—

vb7:3.3
Pali: “atthissa kāye kesā lomā nakhā dantā taco, maṁsaṁ nhāru aṭṭhi aṭṭhimiñjaṁ vakkaṁ, hadayaṁ yakanaṁ kilomakaṁ pihakaṁ papphāsaṁ, antaṁ antaguṇaṁ udariyaṁ karīsaṁ, pittaṁ semhaṁ pubbo lohitaṁ sedo medo, assu vasā kheḷo siṅghāṇikā lasikā muttan”ti. 

vb7:3.4
Pali: So taṁ nimittaṁ āsevati bhāveti bahulīkaroti, svāvatthitaṁ vavatthapeti. 

vb7:3.5
Pali: So taṁ nimittaṁ āsevitvā bhāvetvā bahulīkaritvā svāvatthitaṁ vavatthapetvā ajjhattabahiddhā kāye cittaṁ upasaṁharati. 

vb7:4.1
Pali: Kathañca bhikkhu ajjhattabahiddhā kāye kāyānupassī viharati? 

vb7:4.2
Pali: Idha bhikkhu ajjhattabahiddhā kāyaṁ uddhaṁ pādatalā adho kesamatthakā tacapariyantaṁ pūraṁ nānappakārassa asucino paccavekkhati—

vb7:4.3
Pali: “atthi imasmiṁ kāye kesā lomā nakhā dantā taco, maṁsaṁ nhāru aṭṭhi aṭṭhimiñjaṁ vakkaṁ, hadayaṁ yakanaṁ kilomakaṁ pihakaṁ papphāsaṁ, antaṁ antaguṇaṁ udariyaṁ karīsaṁ, pittaṁ semhaṁ pubbo lohitaṁ sedo medo, assu vasā kheḷo siṅghāṇikā lasikā muttan”ti. 

vb7:4.4
Pali: Evaṁ bhikkhu ajjhattabahiddhā kāye kāyānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaṁ. 

vb7:5.1
Pali: “Anupassī”ti. 

vb7:5.2
Pali: Tattha katamā anupassanā? 

vb7:5.3
Pali: Yā paññā pajānanā …pe… amoho dhammavicayo sammādiṭṭhi—

vb7:5.4
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “anupassanā”. 

vb7:5.5
Pali: Imāya anupassanāya upeto hoti samupeto upāgato samupāgato upapanno sampanno samannāgato. 

vb7:5.6
Pali: Tena vuccati “anupassī”ti. 

vb7:6.1
Pali: “Viharatī”ti. 

vb7:6.2
Pali: Iriyati vattati pāleti yapeti yāpeti carati viharati. 

vb7:6.3
Pali: Tena vuccati “viharatī”ti. 

vb7:7.1
Pali: “Ātāpī”ti. 

vb7:7.2
Pali: Tattha katamo ātāpo? 

vb7:7.3
Pali: Yo cetasiko vīriyārambho …pe… sammāvāyāmo—

vb7:7.4
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “ātāpo”. 

vb7:7.5
Pali: Iminā ātāpena upeto hoti samupeto upāgato samupāgato upapanno sampanno samannāgato. 

vb7:7.6
Pali: Tena vuccati “ātāpī”ti. 

vb7:8.1
Pali: “Sampajāno”ti. 

vb7:8.2
Pali: Tattha katamaṁ sampajaññaṁ? 

vb7:8.3
Pali: Yā paññā pajānanā …pe… amoho dhammavicayo sammādiṭṭhi—

vb7:8.4
Pali: idaṁ vuccati “sampajaññaṁ”. 

vb7:8.5
Pali: Iminā sampajaññena upeto hoti samupeto upāgato samupāgato upapanno sampanno samannāgato. 

vb7:8.6
Pali: Tena vuccati “sampajāno”ti. 

vb7:9.1
Pali: “Satimā”ti. 

vb7:9.2
Pali: Tattha katamā sati? 

vb7:9.3
Pali: Yā sati anussati …pe… sammāsati—

vb7:9.4
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “sati”. 

vb7:9.5
Pali: Imāya satiyā upeto hoti samupeto upāgato samupāgato upapanno sampanno samannāgato. 

vb7:9.6
Pali: Tena vuccati “satimā”ti. 

vb7:10.1
Pali: “Vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassan”ti. 

vb7:10.2
Pali: Tattha katamo loko? 

vb7:10.3
Pali: Sveva kāyo loko. 

vb7:10.4
Pali: Pañcapi upādānakkhandhā loko. 

vb7:10.5
Pali: Ayaṁ vuccati “loko”. 

vb7:10.6
Pali: Tattha katamā abhijjhā? 

vb7:10.7
Pali: Yo rāgo sārāgo …pe… cittassa sārāgo—

vb7:10.8
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “abhijjhā”. 

vb7:10.9
Pali: Tattha katamaṁ domanassaṁ? 

vb7:10.10
Pali: Yaṁ cetasikaṁ asātaṁ cetasikaṁ dukkhaṁ cetosamphassajaṁ asātaṁ dukkhaṁ vedayitaṁ cetosamphassajā asātā dukkhā vedanā—

vb7:10.11
Pali: idaṁ vuccati “domanassaṁ”. 

vb7:10.12
Pali: Iti ayañca abhijjhā idañca domanassaṁ imamhi loke vinītā honti paṭivinītā santā samitā vūpasantā atthaṅgatā abbhatthaṅgatā appitā byappitā sositā visositā byantīkatā. 

vb7:10.13
Pali: Tena vuccati “vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassan”ti. 

vb7:11.1
Pali: Kāyānupassanāniddeso.

vb7:12.2

vb7:12.3

vb7:17.0
Pali: 1.3. Cittānupassanāniddesa 

vb7:17.1
Pali: Kathañca bhikkhu ajjhattaṁ citte cittānupassī viharati? 

vb7:17.2
Pali: Idha bhikkhu sarāgaṁ vā cittaṁ “sarāgaṁ me cittan”ti pajānāti, vītarāgaṁ vā cittaṁ “vītarāgaṁ me cittan”ti pajānāti, sadosaṁ vā cittaṁ “sadosaṁ me cittan”ti pajānāti, vītadosaṁ vā cittaṁ “vītadosaṁ me cittan”ti pajānāti, samohaṁ vā cittaṁ “samohaṁ me cittan”ti pajānāti, vītamohaṁ vā cittaṁ “vītamohaṁ me cittan”ti pajānāti, saṅkhittaṁ vā cittaṁ “saṅkhittaṁ me cittan”ti pajānāti, vikkhittaṁ vā cittaṁ “vikkhittaṁ me cittan”ti pajānāti, mahaggataṁ vā cittaṁ “mahaggataṁ me cittan”ti pajānāti, amahaggataṁ vā cittaṁ “amahaggataṁ me cittan”ti pajānāti, sauttaraṁ vā cittaṁ “sauttaraṁ me cittan”ti pajānāti, anuttaraṁ vā cittaṁ “anuttaraṁ me cittan”ti pajānāti, samāhitaṁ vā cittaṁ “samāhitaṁ me cittan”ti pajānāti, asamāhitaṁ vā cittaṁ “asamāhitaṁ me cittan”ti pajānāti, vimuttaṁ vā cittaṁ “vimuttaṁ me cittan”ti pajānāti, avimuttaṁ vā cittaṁ “avimuttaṁ me cittan”ti pajānāti. 

vb7:17.3
Pali: So taṁ nimittaṁ āsevati bhāveti bahulīkaroti svāvatthitaṁ vavatthapeti. 

vb7:17.4
Pali: So taṁ nimittaṁ āsevitvā bhāvetvā bahulīkaritvā svāvatthitaṁ vavatthapetvā bahiddhā citte cittaṁ upasaṁharati. 

vb7:18.1

vb7:18.2

vb7:18.3
Pali: So taṁ nimittaṁ āsevati bhāveti bahulīkaroti svāvatthitaṁ vavatthapeti. 

vb7:18.4
Pali: So taṁ nimittaṁ āsevitvā bhāvetvā bahulīkaritvā svāvatthitaṁ vavatthapetvā ajjhattabahiddhā citte cittaṁ upasaṁharati. 

vb7:19.1

vb7:19.2

Pali: Tena vuccati “vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassan”ti. 

vb7:21.1
Pali: Cittānupassanāniddeso. 

vb7:22.0
Pali: 1.4. Dhammānupassanāniddesa 

vb7:22.1
Pali: Kathañca bhikkhu ajjhattaṁ dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati? 

vb7:22.2
Pali: Idha bhikkhu santaṁ vā ajjhattaṁ kāmacchandaṁ “atthi me ajjhattaṁ kāmacchando”ti pajānāti, asantaṁ vā ajjhattaṁ kāmacchandaṁ “natthi me ajjhattaṁ kāmacchando”ti pajānāti, yathā ca anuppannassa kāmacchandassa uppādo hoti tañca pajānāti, yathā ca uppannassa kāmacchandassa pahānaṁ hoti tañca pajānāti, yathā ca pahīnassa kāmacchandassa āyatiṁ anuppādo hoti tañca pajānāti. 

vb7:22.3
Pali: Santaṁ vā ajjhattaṁ byāpādaṁ …pe… 

vb7:22.4
Pali: santaṁ vā ajjhattaṁ thinamiddhaṁ …pe… 

vb7:22.5
Pali: santaṁ vā ajjhattaṁ uddhaccakukkuccaṁ …pe… 

vb7:22.6
Pali: santaṁ vā ajjhattaṁ vicikicchaṁ “atthi me ajjhattaṁ vicikicchā”ti pajānāti, asantaṁ vā ajjhattaṁ vicikicchaṁ “natthi me ajjhattaṁ vicikicchā”ti pajānāti, yathā ca anuppannāya vicikicchāya uppādo hoti tañca pajānāti, yathā ca uppannāya vicikicchāya pahānaṁ hoti tañca pajānāti, yathā ca pahīnāya vicikicchāya āyatiṁ anuppādo hoti tañca pajānāti. 

vb7:23.1
Pali: Santaṁ vā ajjhattaṁ satisambojjhaṅgaṁ “atthi me ajjhattaṁ satisambojjhaṅgo”ti pajānāti, asantaṁ vā ajjhattaṁ satisambojjhaṅgaṁ “natthi me ajjhattaṁ satisambojjhaṅgo”ti pajānāti, yathā ca anuppannassa satisambojjhaṅgassa uppādo hoti tañca pajānāti, yathā ca uppannassa satisambojjhaṅgassa bhāvanāya pāripūrī hoti tañca pajānāti, santaṁ vā ajjhattaṁ dhammavicayasambojjhaṅgaṁ …pe… 

vb7:23.2
Pali: santaṁ vā ajjhattaṁ vīriyasambojjhaṅgaṁ …pe… 

vb7:23.3
Pali: santaṁ vā ajjhattaṁ pītisambojjhaṅgaṁ …pe… 

vb7:23.4
Pali: santaṁ vā ajjhattaṁ passaddhisambojjhaṅgaṁ …pe… 

vb7:23.5
Pali: santaṁ vā ajjhattaṁ samādhisambojjhaṅgaṁ …pe… 

vb7:23.6
Pali: santaṁ vā ajjhattaṁ upekkhāsambojjhaṅgaṁ “atthi me ajjhattaṁ upekkhāsambojjhaṅgo”ti pajānāti, asantaṁ vā ajjhattaṁ upekkhāsambojjhaṅgaṁ “natthi me ajjhattaṁ upekkhāsambojjhaṅgo”ti pajānāti, yathā ca anuppannassa upekkhāsambojjhaṅgassa uppādo hoti tañca pajānāti, yathā ca uppannassa upekkhāsambojjhaṅgassa bhāvanāya pāripūrī hoti, tañca pajānāti. 

vb7:23.7
Pali: So taṁ nimittaṁ āsevati bhāveti bahulīkaroti, svāvatthitaṁ vavatthapeti. 

vb7:23.8
Pali: So taṁ nimittaṁ āsevitvā bhāvetvā bahulīkaritvā svāvatthitaṁ vavatthapetvā bahiddhā dhammesu cittaṁ upasaṁharati. 

vb7:24.1
Pali: Kathañca bhikkhu bahiddhā dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati? 

vb7:24.2
Pali: Idha bhikkhu santaṁ vāssa kāmacchandaṁ “atthissa kāmacchando”ti pajānāti, asantaṁ vāssa kāmacchandaṁ “natthissa kāmacchando”ti pajānāti, yathā ca anuppannassa kāmacchandassa uppādo hoti tañca pajānāti, yathā ca uppannassa kāmacchandassa pahānaṁ hoti tañca pajānāti, yathā ca pahīnassa kāmacchandassa āyatiṁ anuppādo hoti tañca pajānāti. 

vb7:24.3
Pali: Santaṁ vāssa byāpādaṁ …pe… 

vb7:24.4
Pali: santaṁ vāssa thinamiddhaṁ …pe… 

vb7:24.5
Pali: santaṁ vāssa uddhaccakukkuccaṁ …pe… 

vb7:24.6
Pali: santaṁ vāssa vicikicchaṁ “atthissa vicikicchā”ti pajānāti, asantaṁ vāssa vicikicchaṁ “natthissa vicikicchā”ti pajānāti, yathā ca anuppannāya vicikicchāya uppādo hoti tañca pajānāti, yathā ca uppannāya vicikicchāya pahānaṁ hoti tañca pajānāti, yathā ca pahīnāya vicikicchāya āyatiṁ anuppādo hoti tañca pajānāti. 

vb7:25.1
Pali: Santaṁ vāssa satisambojjhaṅgaṁ “atthissa satisambojjhaṅgo”ti pajānāti, asantaṁ vāssa satisambojjhaṅgaṁ “natthissa satisambojjhaṅgo”ti pajānāti, yathā ca anuppannassa satisambojjhaṅgassa uppādo hoti tañca pajānāti, yathā ca uppannassa satisambojjhaṅgassa bhāvanāya pāripūrī hoti tañca pajānāti. 

vb7:25.2
Pali: Santaṁ vāssa dhammavicayasambojjhaṅgaṁ …pe… 

vb7:25.3

vb7:25.4
Pali: santaṁ vāssa pītisambojjhaṅgaṁ …pe… 

vb7:25.5
Pali: santaṁ vāssa passaddhisambojjhaṅgaṁ …pe… 

vb7:25.6
Pali: santaṁ vāssa samādhisambojjhaṅgaṁ …pe… 

vb7:25.7
Pali: santaṁ vāssa upekkhāsambojjhaṅgaṁ “atthissa upekkhāsambojjhaṅgo”ti pajānāti, asantaṁ vāssa upekkhāsambojjhaṅgaṁ “natthissa upekkhāsambojjhaṅgo”ti pajānāti, yathā ca anuppannassa upekkhāsambojjhaṅgassa uppādo hoti tañca pajānāti, yathā ca uppannassa upekkhāsambojjhaṅgassa bhāvanāya pāripūrī hoti tañca pajānāti. 

vb7:25.8
Pali: So taṁ nimittaṁ āsevati bhāveti bahulīkaroti, svāvatthitaṁ vavatthapeti. 

vb7:25.9
Pali: So taṁ nimittaṁ āsevitvā bhāvetvā bahulīkaritvā svāvatthitaṁ vavatthapetvā ajjhattabahiddhā dhammesu cittaṁ upasaṁharati. 

vb7:26.1
Pali: Kathañca bhikkhu ajjhattabahiddhā dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati? 

vb7:26.2
Pali: Idha bhikkhu santaṁ vā kāmacchandaṁ “atthi kāmacchando”ti pajānāti, asantaṁ vā kāmacchandaṁ “natthi kāmacchando”ti pajānāti, yathā ca anuppannassa kāmacchandassa uppādo hoti tañca pajānāti, yathā ca uppannassa kāmacchandassa pahānaṁ hoti tañca pajānāti, yathā ca pahīnassa kāmacchandassa āyatiṁ anuppādo hoti tañca pajānāti. 

vb7:26.3
Pali: Santaṁ vā byāpādaṁ …pe… 

vb7:26.4
Pali: santaṁ vā thinamiddhaṁ …pe… 

vb7:26.5
Pali: santaṁ vā uddhaccakukkuccaṁ …pe… 

vb7:26.6
Pali: santaṁ vā vicikicchaṁ “atthi vicikicchā”ti pajānāti, asantaṁ vā vicikicchaṁ “natthi vicikicchā”ti pajānāti, yathā ca anuppannāya vicikicchāya uppādo hoti tañca pajānāti, yathā ca uppannāya vicikicchāya pahānaṁ hoti tañca pajānāti, yathā ca pahīnāya vicikicchāya āyatiṁ anuppādo hoti tañca pajānāti. 

vb7:27.1
Pali: Santaṁ vā satisambojjhaṅgaṁ “atthi satisambojjhaṅgo”ti pajānāti, asantaṁ vā satisambojjhaṅgaṁ “natthi satisambojjhaṅgo”ti pajānāti, yathā ca anuppannassa satisambojjhaṅgassa uppādo hoti tañca pajānāti, yathā ca uppannassa satisambojjhaṅgassa bhāvanāya pāripūrī hoti tañca pajānāti.

vb7:27.7

vb7:27.8
Pali: Evaṁ bhikkhu ajjhattabahiddhā dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaṁ. 

vb7:28.1
Pali: “Anupassī”ti. 

vb7:28.2
Pali: Tattha katamā anupassanā? 

vb7:28.3
Pali: Yā paññā pajānanā …pe… amoho dhammavicayo sammādiṭṭhi—

vb7:28.4
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “anupassanā”. 

vb7:28.5
Pali: Imāya anupassanāya upeto hoti samupeto upāgato samupāgato upapanno sampanno samannāgato. 

vb7:28.6
Pali: Tena vuccati “anupassī”ti. 

vb7:29.1
Pali: “Viharatī”ti. 

vb7:29.2
Pali: Iriyati vattati pāleti yapeti yāpeti carati viharati. 

vb7:29.3
Pali: Tena vuccati “viharatī”ti. 

vb7:30.1
Pali: “Ātāpī”ti. 

vb7:30.2
Pali: Tattha katamo ātāpo? 

vb7:30.3
Pali: Yo cetasiko vīriyārambho …pe… sammāvāyāmo—

vb7:30.4
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “ātāpo”. 

vb7:30.5
Pali: Iminā ātāpena upeto hoti …pe… samannāgato. 

vb7:30.6
Pali: Tena vuccati “ātāpī”ti. 

vb7:31.1
Pali: “Sampajāno”ti. 

vb7:31.2
Pali: Tattha katamaṁ sampajaññaṁ? 

vb7:31.3
Pali: Yā paññā pajānanā …pe… amoho dhammavicayo sammādiṭṭhi—

vb7:31.4
Pali: idaṁ vuccati “sampajaññaṁ”. 

vb7:31.5
Pali: Iminā sampajaññena upeto hoti …pe… samannāgato. 

vb7:31.6
Pali: Tena vuccati “sampajāno”ti. 

vb7:32.1
Pali: “Satimā”ti. 

vb7:32.2
Pali: Tattha katamā sati? 

vb7:32.3
Pali: Yā sati anussati …pe… sammāsati—

vb7:32.4
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “sati”. 

vb7:32.5
Pali: Imāya satiyā upeto hoti …pe… samannāgato. 

vb7:32.6
Pali: Tena vuccati “satimā”ti. 

vb7:33.1
Pali: “Vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassan”ti. 

vb7:33.2
Pali: Tattha katamo loko? 

vb7:33.3
Pali: Teva dhammā loko. 

vb7:33.4
Pali: Pañcapi upādānakkhandhā loko. 

vb7:33.5
Pali: Ayaṁ vuccati “loko”. 

vb7:33.6
Pali: Tattha katamā abhijjhā? 

vb7:33.7
Pali: Yo rāgo sārāgo …pe… cittassa sārāgo—

vb7:33.8
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “abhijjhā”. 

vb7:33.9
Pali: Tattha katamaṁ domanassaṁ? 

vb7:33.10
Pali: Yaṁ cetasikaṁ asātaṁ cetasikaṁ dukkhaṁ cetosamphassajaṁ asātaṁ dukkhaṁ vedayitaṁ cetosamphassajā asātā dukkhā vedanā—

vb7:33.11
Pali: idaṁ vuccati “domanassaṁ”. 

vb7:33.12
Pali: Iti ayañca abhijjhā idañca domanassaṁ imamhi loke vinītā honti paṭivinītā santā samitā vūpasantā atthaṅgatā abbhatthaṅgatā appitā byappitā sositā visositā byantīkatā. 

vb7:33.13
Pali: Tena vuccati “vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassan”ti. 

vb7:34.1
Pali: Dhammānupassanāniddeso. 

vb7:34.2
Pali: Suttantabhājanīyaṁ. 

vb7:35.0
Pali: 2. Abhidhammabhājanīya 

vb7:35.1
Pali: Cattāro satipaṭṭhānā—

vb7:35.2
Pali: idha bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati, vedanāsu vedanānupassī viharati, citte cittānupassī viharati, dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati. 

vb7:36.1
Pali: Kathañca bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati? 

vb7:36.2
Pali: Idha bhikkhu yasmiṁ samaye lokuttaraṁ jhānaṁ bhāveti niyyānikaṁ apacayagāmiṁ diṭṭhigatānaṁ pahānāya paṭhamāya bhūmiyā pattiyā vivicceva kāmehi …pe… paṭhamaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati dukkhapaṭipadaṁ dandhābhiññaṁ kāye kāyānupassī, yā tasmiṁ samaye sati anussati sammāsati satisambojjhaṅgo maggaṅgaṁ maggapariyāpannaṁ—

vb7:36.3
Pali: idaṁ vuccati “satipaṭṭhānaṁ”. 

vb7:36.4
Pali: Avasesā dhammā satipaṭṭhānasampayuttā. 

vb7:37.1
Pali: Kathañca bhikkhu vedanāsu vedanānupassī viharati? 

vb7:37.2
Pali: Idha bhikkhu yasmiṁ samaye lokuttaraṁ jhānaṁ bhāveti niyyānikaṁ apacayagāmiṁ diṭṭhigatānaṁ pahānāya paṭhamāya bhūmiyā pattiyā vivicceva kāmehi …pe… paṭhamaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati dukkhapaṭipadaṁ dandhābhiññaṁ vedanāsu vedanānupassī, yā tasmiṁ samaye sati anussati sammāsati satisambojjhaṅgo maggaṅgaṁ maggapariyāpannaṁ—

vb7:37.3
Pali: idaṁ vuccati “satipaṭṭhānaṁ”. 

vb7:37.4
Pali: Avasesā dhammā satipaṭṭhānasampayuttā. 

vb7:38.1
Pali: Kathañca bhikkhu citte cittānupassī viharati? 

vb7:38.2
Pali: Idha bhikkhu yasmiṁ samaye lokuttaraṁ jhānaṁ bhāveti niyyānikaṁ apacayagāmiṁ diṭṭhigatānaṁ pahānāya paṭhamāya bhūmiyā pattiyā vivicceva kāmehi …pe… paṭhamaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati dukkhapaṭipadaṁ dandhābhiññaṁ citte cittānupassī, yā tasmiṁ samaye sati anussati sammāsati satisambojjhaṅgo maggaṅgaṁ maggapariyāpannaṁ—

vb7:38.3
Pali: idaṁ vuccati “satipaṭṭhānaṁ”. 

vb7:38.4
Pali: Avasesā dhammā satipaṭṭhānasampayuttā. 

vb7:39.1
Pali: Kathañca bhikkhu dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati? 

vb7:39.2
Pali: Idha bhikkhu yasmiṁ samaye lokuttaraṁ jhānaṁ bhāveti niyyānikaṁ apacayagāmiṁ diṭṭhigatānaṁ pahānāya paṭhamāya bhūmiyā pattiyā vivicceva kāmehi …pe… paṭhamaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati dukkhapaṭipadaṁ dandhābhiññaṁ dhammesu dhammānupassī, yā tasmiṁ samaye sati anussati sammāsati satisambojjhaṅgo maggaṅgaṁ maggapariyāpannaṁ—

vb7:39.4
Pali: Avasesā dhammā satipaṭṭhānasampayuttā. 

vb7:40.1
Pali: Tattha katamaṁ satipaṭṭhānaṁ? 

vb7:40.2
Pali: Idha bhikkhu yasmiṁ samaye lokuttaraṁ jhānaṁ bhāveti niyyānikaṁ apacayagāmiṁ diṭṭhigatānaṁ pahānāya paṭhamāya bhūmiyā pattiyā vivicceva kāmehi …pe… paṭhamaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati dukkhapaṭipadaṁ dandhābhiññaṁ dhammesu dhammānupassī, yā tasmiṁ samaye sati anussati sammāsati satisambojjhaṅgo maggaṅgaṁ maggapariyāpannaṁ—

vb7:42.1
Pali: Kathañca bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati? 

vb7:42.2

vb7:42.3
Pali: Ime dhammā kusalā. 

vb7:42.4
Pali: Tasseva lokuttarassa kusalassa jhānassa katattā bhāvitattā vipākaṁ vivicceva kāmehi …pe… paṭhamaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati dukkhapaṭipadaṁ dandhābhiññaṁ suññataṁ kāye kāyānupassī, yā tasmiṁ samaye sati anussati sammāsati satisambojjhaṅgo maggaṅgaṁ maggapariyāpannaṁ—

vb7:42.5
Pali: idaṁ vuccati “satipaṭṭhānaṁ”.

Pali: Ime dhammā kusalā. 

vb7:45.4
Pali: Tasseva lokuttarassa kusalassa jhānassa katattā bhāvitattā vipākaṁ vivicceva kāmehi …pe… paṭhamaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati dukkhapaṭipadaṁ dandhābhiññaṁ suññataṁ dhammesu dhammānupassī, yā tasmiṁ samaye sati anussati sammāsati satisambojjhaṅgo maggaṅgaṁ maggapariyāpannaṁ—

vb7:45.5
Pali: idaṁ vuccati “satipaṭṭhānaṁ”. 

vb7:45.6
Pali: Avasesā dhammā satipaṭṭhānasampayuttā. 

vb7:46.1
Pali: Tattha katamaṁ satipaṭṭhānaṁ? 

vb7:46.2
Pali: Idha bhikkhu yasmiṁ samaye lokuttaraṁ jhānaṁ bhāveti niyyānikaṁ apacayagāmiṁ diṭṭhigatānaṁ pahānāya paṭhamāya bhūmiyā pattiyā vivicceva kāmehi …pe… paṭhamaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati dukkhapaṭipadaṁ dandhābhiññaṁ, tasmiṁ samaye phasso hoti …pe… avikkhepo hoti. 

vb7:46.3
Pali: Ime dhammā kusalā. 

vb7:46.4
Pali: Tasseva lokuttarassa kusalassa jhānassa katattā bhāvitattā vipākaṁ vivicceva kāmehi …pe… paṭhamaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati dukkhapaṭipadaṁ dandhābhiññaṁ suññataṁ, yā tasmiṁ samaye sati anussati sammāsati satisambojjhaṅgo maggaṅgaṁ maggapariyāpannaṁ—

vb7:46.5
Pali: idaṁ vuccati “satipaṭṭhānaṁ”. 

vb7:46.6
Pali: Avasesā dhammā satipaṭṭhānasampayuttā. 

vb7:47.1
Pali: Abhidhammabhājanīyaṁ. 

vb7:48.0
Pali: 3. Pañhāpucchaka 

vb7:48.1
Pali: Cattāro satipaṭṭhānā—

vb7:48.2
Pali: idha bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaṁ, vedanāsu vedanānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaṁ, citte cittānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaṁ, dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaṁ. 

vb7:49.1
Pali: Catunnaṁ satipaṭṭhānānaṁ kati kusalā, kati akusalā, kati abyākatā …pe… kati saraṇā, kati araṇā? 

vb7:50.0
Pali: 3.1. Tika 

vb7:50.1
Pali: Siyā kusalā, siyā abyākatā …pe…. 

vb7:50.2
Pali: Siyā sukhāya vedanāya sampayuttā, siyā adukkhamasukhāya vedanāya sampayuttā.

Pali: Siyā vipākā siyā vipākadhammadhammā. 

vb7:50.4
Pali: Anupādinnaanupādāniyā.

Pali: Asaṅkiliṭṭhaasaṅkilesikā.

vb7:50.7
Pali: Siyā pītisahagatā, siyā sukhasahagatā, siyā upekkhāsahagatā. 

vb7:50.8
Pali: Neva dassanena na bhāvanāya pahātabbā. 

vb7:50.9
Pali: Neva dassanena na bhāvanāya pahātabbahetukā. 

vb7:50.10
Pali: Siyā apacayagāmino, siyā nevācayagāmināpacayagāmino. 

vb7:50.11

vb7:50.12
Pali: Appamāṇā.

vb7:50.15

vb7:50.16

vb7:50.17
Pali: Siyā uppannā, siyā anuppannā, siyā uppādino. 

vb7:50.18
Pali: Siyā atītā, siyā anāgatā, siyā paccuppannā. 

vb7:50.19

vb7:50.20
Pali: Siyā ajjhattā, siyā bahiddhā, siyā ajjhattabahiddhā. 

vb7:50.21
Pali: Bahiddhārammaṇā. 

vb7:50.22

vb8:1.1
Pali: Cattāro sammappadhānā—

vb8:1.2
Pali: idha bhikkhu anuppannānaṁ pāpakānaṁ akusalānaṁ dhammānaṁ anuppādāya chandaṁ janeti vāyamati vīriyaṁ ārabhati cittaṁ paggaṇhāti padahati, uppannānaṁ pāpakānaṁ akusalānaṁ dhammānaṁ pahānāya chandaṁ janeti vāyamati vīriyaṁ ārabhati cittaṁ paggaṇhāti padahati, anuppannānaṁ kusalānaṁ dhammānaṁ uppādāya chandaṁ janeti vāyamati vīriyaṁ ārabhati cittaṁ paggaṇhāti padahati, uppannānaṁ kusalānaṁ dhammānaṁ ṭhitiyā asammosāya bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya bhāvanāya pāripūriyā chandaṁ janeti vāyamati vīriyaṁ ārabhati cittaṁ paggaṇhāti padahati. 

vb8:2.1
Pali: Kathañca bhikkhu anuppannānaṁ pāpakānaṁ akusalānaṁ dhammānaṁ anuppādāya chandaṁ janeti vāyamati vīriyaṁ ārabhati cittaṁ paggaṇhāti padahati? 

vb8:2.2
Pali: Tattha katame anuppannā pāpakā akusalā dhammā? 

vb8:2.3
Pali: Tīṇi akusalamūlāni—

vb8:2.4
Pali: lobho, doso, moho. 

vb8:2.5
Pali: Tadekaṭṭhā ca kilesā.

vb8:2.9

Pali: Iddhipādavibhaṅga 

vb9:1.0
Pali: 1. Suttantabhājanīya 

vb9:1.1
Pali: Cattāro iddhipādā—

vb9:1.2
Pali: idha bhikkhu chandasamādhipadhānasaṅkhārasamannāgataṁ iddhipādaṁ bhāveti, 

vb9:1.3
Pali: vīriyasamādhipadhānasaṅkhārasamannāgataṁ iddhipādaṁ bhāveti, 

vb9:1.4
Pali: cittasamādhipadhānasaṅkhārasamannāgataṁ iddhipādaṁ bhāveti, 

vb9:1.5
Pali: vīmaṁsāsamādhipadhānasaṅkhārasamannāgataṁ iddhipādaṁ bhāveti. 

vb9:2.0
Pali: 1.1. Chandiddhipāda 

vb9:2.1
Pali: Kathañca bhikkhu chandasamādhipadhānasaṅkhārasamannāgataṁ iddhipādaṁ bhāveti? 

vb9:2.2
Pali: Chandañce bhikkhu adhipatiṁ karitvā labhati samādhiṁ, labhati cittassekaggataṁ—

vb9:2.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “chandasamādhi”. 

vb9:2.4
Pali: So anuppannānaṁ pāpakānaṁ akusalānaṁ dhammānaṁ anuppādāya chandaṁ janeti vāyamati vīriyaṁ ārabhati cittaṁ paggaṇhāti padahati, uppannānaṁ pāpakānaṁ akusalānaṁ dhammānaṁ pahānāya chandaṁ janeti vāyamati vīriyaṁ ārabhati cittaṁ paggaṇhāti padahati, anuppannānaṁ kusalānaṁ dhammānaṁ uppādāya chandaṁ janeti vāyamati vīriyaṁ ārabhati cittaṁ paggaṇhāti padahati, uppannānaṁ kusalānaṁ dhammānaṁ ṭhitiyā asammosāya bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya bhāvanāya pāripūriyā chandaṁ janeti vāyamati vīriyaṁ ārabhati cittaṁ paggaṇhāti padahati. 

vb9:2.5
Pali: Ime vuccanti “padhānasaṅkhārā”. 

vb9:2.6
Pali: Iti ayañca chandasamādhi, ime ca padhānasaṅkhārā. 

vb9:2.7
Pali: Tadekajjhaṁ abhisaññūhitvā abhisaṅkhipitvā chandasamādhipadhānasaṅkhārotveva saṅkhyaṁ gacchati. 

vb9:3.1
Pali: Tattha katamo chando? 

vb9:3.2
Pali: Yo chando chandikatā kattukamyatā kusalo dhammacchando—

vb9:3.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “chando”. 

vb9:4.1
Pali: Tattha katamo samādhi? 

vb9:4.2
Pali: Yā cittassa ṭhiti saṇṭhiti avaṭṭhiti avisāhāro avikkhepo avisāhaṭamānasatā samatho samādhindriyaṁ samādhibalaṁ sammāsamādhi—

vb9:4.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “samādhi”. 

vb9:5.1
Pali: Tattha katamo padhānasaṅkhāro? 

vb9:5.2
Pali: Yo cetasiko vīriyārambho nikkamo parakkamo uyyāmo vāyāmo ussāho ussoḷhī thāmo ṭhiti asithilaparakkamatā anikkhittachandatā anikkhittadhuratā dhurasampaggāho vīriyaṁ vīriyindriyaṁ vīriyabalaṁ sammāvāyāmo—

vb9:5.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “padhānasaṅkhāro”. 

vb9:5.4
Pali: Iti iminā ca chandena, iminā ca samādhinā, iminā ca padhānasaṅkhārena upeto hoti samupeto upāgato samupāgato upapanno sampanno samannāgato. 

vb9:5.5
Pali: Tena vuccati “chandasamādhipadhānasaṅkhārasamannāgato”ti. 

vb9:6.1
Pali: “Iddhī”ti. 

vb9:6.2
Pali: Yā tesaṁ dhammānaṁ iddhi samiddhi ijjhanā samijjhanā lābho paṭilābho patti sampatti phusanā sacchikiriyā upasampadā. 

vb9:7.1
Pali: “Iddhipādo”ti. 

vb9:7.2
Pali: Tathābhūtassa vedanākkhandho, saññākkhandho, saṅkhārakkhandho, viññāṇakkhandho. 

vb9:8.1
Pali: “Iddhipādaṁ bhāvetī”ti. 

vb9:8.2
Pali: Te dhamme āsevati bhāveti bahulīkaroti. 

vb9:8.3
Pali: Tena vuccati “iddhipādaṁ bhāvetī”ti.

vb9:32.2
Pali: Idha bhikkhu yasmiṁ samaye lokuttaraṁ jhānaṁ bhāveti niyyānikaṁ apacayagāmiṁ diṭṭhigatānaṁ pahānāya paṭhamāya bhūmiyā pattiyā vivicceva kāmehi …pe… paṭhamaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati dukkhapaṭipadaṁ dandhābhiññaṁ, tasmiṁ samaye chandasamādhipadhānasaṅkhārasamannāgataṁ iddhipādaṁ bhāveti.

vb9:53.2
Pali: Idha bhikkhu yasmiṁ samaye lokuttaraṁ jhānaṁ bhāveti niyyānikaṁ apacayagāmiṁ diṭṭhigatānaṁ pahānāya paṭhamāya bhūmiyā pattiyā vivicceva kāmehi …pe… paṭhamaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati dukkhapaṭipadaṁ dandhābhiññaṁ, tasmiṁ samaye vīmaṁsāsamādhipadhānasaṅkhārasamannāgataṁ iddhipādaṁ bhāveti. 

vb9:54.1
Pali: Tattha katamā vīmaṁsā? 

vb9:54.2
Pali: Yā paññā pajānanā …pe… amoho dhammavicayo sammādiṭṭhi dhammavicayasambojjhaṅgo maggaṅgaṁ maggapariyāpannaṁ—

vb9:54.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “vīmaṁsā”. 

vb9:55.1
Pali: Tattha katamo samādhi? 

vb9:55.2
Pali: Yā cittassa ṭhiti saṇṭhiti …pe… sammāsamādhi samādhisambojjhaṅgo maggaṅgaṁ maggapariyāpannaṁ—

vb9:55.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “samādhi”. 

vb9:56.1
Pali: Tattha katamo padhānasaṅkhāro? 

vb9:56.2
Pali: Yo cetasiko vīriyārambho …pe… sammāvāyāmo vīriyasambojjhaṅgo maggaṅgaṁ maggapariyāpannaṁ—

vb9:56.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “padhānasaṅkhāro”. 

vb9:56.4
Pali: Iti imāya ca vīmaṁsāya, iminā ca samādhinā, iminā ca padhānasaṅkhārena upeto hoti samupeto upāgato samupāgato upapanno sampanno samannāgato. 

vb9:56.5
Pali: Tena vuccati “vīmaṁsāsamādhipadhānasaṅkhārasamannāgato”ti 

vb9:57.1
Pali: “Iddhī”ti. 

vb9:57.2
Pali: Yā tesaṁ dhammānaṁ iddhi samiddhi ijjhanā samijjhanā lābho paṭilābho patti sampatti phusanā sacchikiriyā upasampadā. 

vb9:58.1
Pali: “Iddhipādo”ti. 

vb9:58.2
Pali: Tathābhūtassa phasso …pe… paggāho avikkhepo. 

vb9:59.1
Pali: “Iddhipādaṁ bhāvetī”ti. 

vb9:59.2
Pali: Te dhamme āsevati bhāveti bahulīkaroti. 

vb9:59.3
Pali: Tena vuccati “iddhipādaṁ bhāvetī”ti. 

vb9:60.1
Pali: Cattāro iddhipādā—

vb9:60.2
Pali: chandiddhipādo, vīriyiddhipādo, cittiddhipādo, vīmaṁsiddhipādo. 

vb9:61.1
Pali: Tattha katamo chandiddhipādo? 

vb9:61.2
Pali: Idha bhikkhu yasmiṁ samaye lokuttaraṁ jhānaṁ bhāveti niyyānikaṁ apacayagāmiṁ diṭṭhigatānaṁ pahānāya paṭhamāya bhūmiyā pattiyā vivicceva kāmehi …pe… paṭhamaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati dukkhapaṭipadaṁ dandhābhiññaṁ, yo tasmiṁ samaye chando chandikatā kattukamyatā kusalo dhammacchando—

vb9:61.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “chandiddhipādo”. 

vb9:61.4
Pali: Avasesā dhammā chandiddhipādasampayuttā. 

vb9:62.1
Pali: Tattha katamo vīriyiddhipādo? 

vb9:62.2
Pali: Idha bhikkhu yasmiṁ samaye lokuttaraṁ jhānaṁ bhāveti niyyānikaṁ apacayagāmiṁ diṭṭhigatānaṁ pahānāya paṭhamāya bhūmiyā pattiyā vivicceva kāmehi …pe… paṭhamaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati dukkhapaṭipadaṁ dandhābhiññaṁ, yo tasmiṁ samaye cetasiko vīriyārambho …pe… sammāvāyāmo vīriyasambojjhaṅgo maggaṅgaṁ maggapariyāpannaṁ—

vb9:62.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “vīriyiddhipādo”. 

vb9:62.4
Pali: Avasesā dhammā vīriyiddhipādasampayuttā. 

vb9:63.1
Pali: Tattha katamo cittiddhipādo? 

vb9:63.2
Pali: Idha bhikkhu yasmiṁ samaye lokuttaraṁ jhānaṁ bhāveti niyyānikaṁ apacayagāmiṁ diṭṭhigatānaṁ pahānāya paṭhamāya bhūmiyā pattiyā vivicceva kāmehi …pe… paṭhamaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati dukkhapaṭipadaṁ dandhābhiññaṁ, yaṁ tasmiṁ samaye cittaṁ mano mānasaṁ …pe… tajjāmanoviññāṇadhātu—

vb9:63.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “cittiddhipādo”. 

vb9:63.4
Pali: Avasesā dhammā cittiddhipādasampayuttā. 

vb9:64.1
Pali: Tattha katamo vīmaṁsiddhipādo? 

vb9:64.2
Pali: Idha bhikkhu yasmiṁ samaye lokuttaraṁ jhānaṁ bhāveti niyyānikaṁ apacayagāmiṁ diṭṭhigatānaṁ pahānāya paṭhamāya bhūmiyā pattiyā vivicceva kāmehi …pe… paṭhamaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati dukkhapaṭipadaṁ dandhābhiññaṁ, yā tasmiṁ samaye paññā pajānanā …pe… amoho dhammavicayo sammādiṭṭhi dhammavicayasambojjhaṅgo maggaṅgaṁ maggapariyāpannaṁ—

vb9:64.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “vīmaṁsiddhipādo”. 

vb9:64.4
Pali: Avasesā dhammā vīmaṁsiddhipādasampayuttā. 

vb9:65.1
Pali: Abhidhammabhājanīyaṁ. 

vb9:66.0
Pali: 3. Pañhāpucchaka 

vb9:66.1
Pali: Cattāro iddhipādā—

vb9:66.2
Pali: idha bhikkhu chandasamādhipadhānasaṅkhārasamannāgataṁ iddhipādaṁ bhāveti, vīriyasamādhi …pe… 

vb9:66.3
Pali: cittasamādhi …pe… 

vb9:66.4
Pali: vīmaṁsāsamādhipadhānasaṅkhārasamannāgataṁ iddhipādaṁ bhāveti. 

vb9:67.1
Pali: Catunnaṁ iddhipādānaṁ kati kusalā, kati akusalā, kati abyākatā …pe… kati saraṇā, kati araṇā? 

vb9:68.0
Pali: 3.1. Tika 

vb9:68.1
Pali: Kusalāyeva. 

vb9:69.1
Pali: Siyā sukhāya vedanāya sampayuttā, siyā adukkhamasukhāya vedanāya sampayuttā. 

vb9:70.1
Pali: Vipākadhammadhammā. 

vb9:71.1
Pali: Anupādinnaanupādāniyā. 

vb9:72.1
Pali: Asaṅkiliṭṭhaasaṅkilesikā. 

vb9:73.1
Pali: Siyā savitakkasavicārā, siyā avitakkavicāramattā, siyā avitakkaavicārā. 

vb9:74.1
Pali: Siyā pītisahagatā, siyā sukhasahagatā, siyā upekkhāsahagatā. 

vb9:75.1
Pali: Neva dassanena na bhāvanāya pahātabbā. 

vb9:76.1
Pali: Neva dassanena na bhāvanāya pahātabbahetukā. 

vb9:77.1
Pali: Apacayagāmino. 

vb9:78.1
Pali: Sekkhā. 

vb9:79.1
Pali: Appamāṇā. 

vb9:80.1
Pali: Appamāṇārammaṇā. 

vb9:81.1
Pali: Paṇītā. 

vb9:82.1
Pali: Sammattaniyatā. 

vb9:83.1
Pali: Na maggārammaṇā, maggahetukā, na maggādhipatino. 

vb9:84.1
Pali: Siyā uppannā, siyā anuppannā, na vattabbā uppādinoti. 

vb9:85.1
Pali: Siyā atītā, siyā anāgatā, siyā paccuppannā. 

vb9:86.1
Pali: Na vattabbā atītārammaṇātipi, anāgatārammaṇātipi, paccuppannārammaṇātipi. 

vb9:87.1
Pali: Siyā ajjhattā, siyā bahiddhā, siyā ajjhattabahiddhā. 

vb9:88.1
Pali: Bahiddhārammaṇā. 

vb9:89.1
Pali: Anidassanaappaṭighā. 

vb9:90.0.1
Pali: 3.2. 3.2 Duka 

vb9:90.0.2
Pali: 3.2.1. Hetugocchaka 

vb9:90.1
Pali: Vīmaṁsiddhipādo hetu, tayo iddhipādā na hetū. 

vb9:90.2
Pali: Sahetukā. 

vb9:90.3
Pali: Hetusampayuttā. 

vb9:90.4
Pali: Vīmaṁsiddhipādo hetu ceva sahetuko ca, tayo iddhipādā na vattabbā “hetū ceva sahetukā cā”ti, sahetukā ceva na ca hetū. 

vb9:90.5
Pali: Vīmaṁsiddhipādo hetu ceva hetusampayutto ca, tayo iddhipādā na vattabbā “hetū ceva hetusampayuttā cā”ti, hetusampayuttā ceva na ca hetū. 

vb9:90.6
Pali: Tayo iddhipādā na hetū sahetukā, vīmaṁsiddhipādo na vattabbo “na hetu sahetuko”tipi, “na hetu ahetuko”tipi. 

vb9:91.0

Pali: Saṅkhatā. 

vb9:91.3
Pali: Anidassanā.

Pali: Appaṭighā. 

vb9:91.5
Pali: Arūpā. 

vb9:91.6
Pali: Lokuttarā. 

vb9:91.7
Pali: Kenaci viññeyyā, kenaci na viññeyyā. 

vb9:91.8
Pali: No āsavā. 

vb9:91.9
Pali: Anāsavā. 

vb9:91.10
Pali: Āsavavippayuttā. 

vb9:91.11

vb9:91.12
Pali: Na vattabbā āsavā ceva āsavasampayuttā cātipi, āsavasampayuttā ceva no ca āsavātipi. 

vb9:91.13

vb9:92.10

vb9:92.14

vb9:92.15
Pali: Tayo iddhipādā cittasaṁsaṭṭhasamuṭṭhānā, cittiddhipādo no cittasaṁsaṭṭhasamuṭṭhāno. 

vb9:92.16

vb9:92.18

vb10:0.1
Pali: Vibhaṅga 

vb10:0.2
Pali: Bojjhaṅgavibhaṅga 

vb10:1.0
Pali: 1. Suttantabhājanīya 

vb10:1.1
Pali: Satta bojjhaṅgā—

vb10:1.2
Pali: satisambojjhaṅgo, dhammavicayasambojjhaṅgo, vīriyasambojjhaṅgo, pītisambojjhaṅgo, passaddhisambojjhaṅgo, samādhisambojjhaṅgo, upekkhāsambojjhaṅgo. 

vb10:2.1
Pali: Tattha katamo satisambojjhaṅgo? 

vb10:2.2
Pali: Idha bhikkhu satimā hoti paramena satinepakkena samannāgato, cirakatampi cirabhāsitampi saritā hoti anussaritā—

vb10:2.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “satisambojjhaṅgo”. 

vb10:3.1
Pali: So tathā sato viharanto taṁ dhammaṁ paññāya pavicinati pavicarati parivīmaṁsamāpajjati—

vb10:3.2
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “dhammavicayasambojjhaṅgo”. 

vb10:4.1
Pali: Tassa taṁ dhammaṁ paññāya pavicinato pavicarato parivīmaṁsamāpajjato āraddhaṁ hoti vīriyaṁ asallīnaṁ—

vb10:4.2
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “vīriyasambojjhaṅgo”. 

vb10:5.1
Pali: Āraddhavīriyassa uppajjati pīti nirāmisā—

vb10:5.2
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “pītisambojjhaṅgo”. 

vb10:6.1
Pali: Pītimanassa kāyopi passambhati, cittampi passambhati—

vb10:6.2
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “passaddhisambojjhaṅgo”. 

vb10:7.1
Pali: Passaddhakāyassa sukhino cittaṁ samādhiyati—

vb10:7.2
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “samādhisambojjhaṅgo”. 

vb10:8.1
Pali: So tathā samāhitaṁ cittaṁ sādhukaṁ ajjhupekkhitā hoti—

vb10:8.2
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “upekkhāsambojjhaṅgo”. 

vb10:9.1
Pali: Satta bojjhaṅgā—

vb10:9.2
Pali: satisambojjhaṅgo, dhammavicayasambojjhaṅgo, vīriyasambojjhaṅgo, pītisambojjhaṅgo, passaddhisambojjhaṅgo, samādhisambojjhaṅgo, upekkhāsambojjhaṅgo. 

vb10:10.1
Pali: Tattha katamo satisambojjhaṅgo? 

vb10:10.2
Pali: Atthi ajjhattaṁ dhammesu sati, atthi bahiddhā dhammesu sati. 

vb10:10.3
Pali: Yadapi ajjhattaṁ dhammesu sati tadapi satisambojjhaṅgo abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saṁvattati. 

vb10:10.4
Pali: Yadapi bahiddhā dhammesu sati tadapi satisambojjhaṅgo abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saṁvattati. 

vb10:11.1
Pali: Tattha katamo dhammavicayasambojjhaṅgo? 

vb10:11.2
Pali: Atthi ajjhattaṁ dhammesu pavicayo, atthi bahiddhā dhammesu pavicayo. 

vb10:11.3
Pali: Yadapi ajjhattaṁ dhammesu pavicayo tadapi dhammavicayasambojjhaṅgo abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saṁvattati. 

vb10:11.4
Pali: Yadapi bahiddhā dhammesu pavicayo tadapi dhammavicayasambojjhaṅgo abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saṁvattati. 

vb10:12.1
Pali: Tattha katamo vīriyasambojjhaṅgo? 

vb10:12.2
Pali: Atthi kāyikaṁ vīriyaṁ, atthi cetasikaṁ vīriyaṁ. 

vb10:12.3
Pali: Yadapi kāyikaṁ vīriyaṁ tadapi vīriyasambojjhaṅgo abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saṁvattati. 

vb10:12.4
Pali: Yadapi cetasikaṁ vīriyaṁ tadapi vīriyasambojjhaṅgo abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saṁvattati. 

vb10:13.1
Pali: Tattha katamo pītisambojjhaṅgo? 

vb10:13.2
Pali: Atthi savitakkasavicārā pīti, atthi avitakkaavicārā pīti. 

vb10:13.3
Pali: Yadapi savitakkasavicārā pīti tadapi pītisambojjhaṅgo abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saṁvattati. 

vb10:13.4
Pali: Yadapi avitakkaavicārā pīti tadapi pītisambojjhaṅgo abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saṁvattati. 

vb10:14.1
Pali: Tattha katamo passaddhisambojjhaṅgo? 

vb10:14.2
Pali: Atthi kāyapassaddhi, atthi cittapassaddhi. 

vb10:14.3
Pali: Yadapi kāyapassaddhi tadapi passaddhisambojjhaṅgo abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saṁvattati. 

vb10:14.4
Pali: Yadapi cittapassaddhi tadapi passaddhisambojjhaṅgo abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saṁvattati. 

vb10:15.1
Pali: Tattha katamo samādhisambojjhaṅgo? 

vb10:15.2
Pali: Atthi savitakko savicāro samādhi, atthi avitakko avicāro samādhi. 

vb10:15.3
Pali: Yadapi savitakko savicāro samādhi tadapi samādhisambojjhaṅgo abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saṁvattati. 

vb10:15.4
Pali: Yadapi avitakko avicāro samādhi tadapi samādhisambojjhaṅgo abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saṁvattati. 

vb10:16.1
Pali: Tattha katamo upekkhāsambojjhaṅgo? 

vb10:16.2
Pali: Atthi ajjhattaṁ dhammesu upekkhā, atthi bahiddhā dhammesu upekkhā. 

vb10:16.3
Pali: Yadapi ajjhattaṁ dhammesu upekkhā tadapi upekkhāsambojjhaṅgo abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saṁvattati. 

vb10:16.4
Pali: Yadapi bahiddhā dhammesu upekkhā tadapi upekkhāsambojjhaṅgo abhiññāya sambodhāya nibbānāya saṁvattati. 

vb10:17.1
Pali: Satta bojjhaṅgā—

vb10:17.2
Pali: satisambojjhaṅgo, dhammavicayasambojjhaṅgo, vīriyasambojjhaṅgo, pītisambojjhaṅgo, passaddhisambojjhaṅgo, samādhisambojjhaṅgo, upekkhāsambojjhaṅgo. 

vb10:18.1
Pali: Tattha katamo satisambojjhaṅgo? 

vb10:18.2
Pali: Idha bhikkhu satisambojjhaṅgaṁ bhāveti vivekanissitaṁ virāganissitaṁ nirodhanissitaṁ vossaggapariṇāmiṁ, 

vb10:18.3
Pali: dhammavicayasambojjhaṅgaṁ bhāveti …pe… 

vb10:18.4
Pali: vīriyasambojjhaṅgaṁ bhāveti … 

vb10:18.5

vb10:18.6

vb10:19.1
Pali: Suttantabhājanīyaṁ. 

vb10:20.0
Pali: 2. Abhidhammabhājanīya 

vb10:20.1
Pali: Satta bojjhaṅgā—

vb10:20.2

Pali: 3. Pañhāpucchaka 

vb10:40.1
Pali: Satta bojjhaṅgā—

vb10:40.2
Pali: satisambojjhaṅgo, dhammavicayasambojjhaṅgo, vīriyasambojjhaṅgo, pītisambojjhaṅgo, passaddhisambojjhaṅgo, samādhisambojjhaṅgo, upekkhāsambojjhaṅgo. 

vb10:41.1
Pali: Sattannaṁ bojjhaṅgānaṁ kati kusalā, kati akusalā, kati abyākatā …pe… kati saraṇā, kati araṇā? 

vb10:42.0
Pali: 3.1. Tika 

vb10:42.1
Pali: Siyā kusalā, siyā abyākatā. 

vb10:43.1
Pali: Pītisambojjhaṅgo sukhāya vedanāya sampayutto; 

vb10:43.2
Pali: cha bojjhaṅgā siyā sukhāya vedanāya sampayuttā, siyā adukkhamasukhāya vedanāya sampayuttā. 

vb10:44.1
Pali: Siyā vipākā, siyā vipākadhammadhammā. 

vb10:45.1
Pali: Anupādinnaanupādāniyā. 

vb10:46.1
Pali: Asaṅkiliṭṭhaasaṅkilesikā. 

vb10:47.1
Pali: Siyā savitakkasavicārā, siyā avitakkavicāramattā, siyā avitakkaavicārā. 

vb10:48.1
Pali: Pītisambojjhaṅgo na pītisahagato, sukhasahagato, na upekkhāsahagato; 

vb10:48.2
Pali: cha bojjhaṅgā siyā pītisahagatā, siyā sukhasahagatā, siyā upekkhāsahagatā. 

vb10:49.1
Pali: Neva dassanena na bhāvanāya pahātabbā. 

vb10:50.1
Pali: Neva dassanena na bhāvanāya pahātabbahetukā. 

vb10:51.1
Pali: Siyā apacayagāmino, siyā nevācayagāmināpacayagāmino. 

vb10:52.1
Pali: Siyā sekkhā, siyā asekkhā. 

vb10:53.1
Pali: Appamāṇā. 

vb10:54.1
Pali: Appamāṇārammaṇā. 

vb10:55.1
Pali: Paṇītā. 

vb10:56.1
Pali: Siyā sammattaniyatā, siyā aniyatā. 

vb10:57.1
Pali: Na maggārammaṇā, siyā maggahetukā, siyā maggādhipatino; 

vb10:57.2
Pali: siyā na vattabbā “maggahetukā”tipi, “maggādhipatino”tipi. 

vb10:58.1
Pali: Siyā uppannā, siyā anuppannā, siyā uppādino. 

vb10:59.1
Pali: Siyā atītā, siyā anāgatā, siyā paccuppannā. 

vb10:60.1
Pali: Na vattabbā “atītārammaṇā”tipi, “anāgatārammaṇā”tipi, “paccuppannārammaṇā”tipi. 

vb10:61.1
Pali: Siyā ajjhattā, siyā bahiddhā, siyā ajjhattabahiddhā. 

vb10:62.1
Pali: Bahiddhārammaṇā. 

vb10:63.1
Pali: Anidassanaappaṭighā. 

vb10:64.0.1
Pali: 3.2. 3.2 Duka 

vb10:64.0.2
Pali: 3.2.1. Hetugocchaka 

vb10:64.1
Pali: Dhammavicayasambojjhaṅgo hetu, cha bojjhaṅgā hetusampayuttā. 

vb10:64.2
Pali: Dhammavicayasambojjhaṅgo hetu ceva sahetuko ca, cha bojjhaṅgā na vattabbā “hetū ceva sahetukā cā”ti, sahetukā ceva na ca hetū. 

vb10:64.3
Pali: Dhammavicayasambojjhaṅgo hetu ceva hetusampayutto ca, cha bojjhaṅgā na vattabbā “hetū ceva hetusampayuttā cā”ti, hetusampayuttā ceva na ca hetū. 

vb10:64.4
Pali: Cha bojjhaṅgā na hetū sahetukā, dhammavicayasambojjhaṅgo na vattabbo “na hetusahetuko”tipi, “na hetuahetuko”tipi.

vb11:0.1
Pali: Vibhaṅga 

vb11:0.2
Pali: Maggaṅgavibhaṅga 

vb11:1.0
Pali: 1. Suttantabhājanīya 

vb11:1.1
Pali: Ariyo aṭṭhaṅgiko maggo, seyyathidaṁ—

vb11:1.2
Pali: sammādiṭṭhi, sammāsaṅkappo, sammāvācā, sammākammanto, sammāājīvo, sammāvāyāmo, sammāsati, sammāsamādhi. 

vb11:2.1
Pali: Tattha katamā sammādiṭṭhi? 

vb11:2.2
Pali: Dukkhe ñāṇaṁ, dukkhasamudaye ñāṇaṁ, dukkhanirodhe ñāṇaṁ, dukkhanirodhagāminiyā paṭipadāya ñāṇaṁ—

vb11:2.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “sammādiṭṭhi”. 

vb11:3.1
Pali: Tattha katamo sammāsaṅkappo? 

vb11:3.2
Pali: Nekkhammasaṅkappo, abyāpādasaṅkappo, avihiṁsāsaṅkappo—

vb11:3.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “sammāsaṅkappo”. 

vb11:4.1
Pali: Tattha katamā sammāvācā? 

vb11:4.2
Pali: Musāvādā veramaṇī, pisuṇāya vācāya veramaṇī, pharusāya vācāya veramaṇī, samphappalāpā veramaṇī—

vb11:4.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “sammāvācā”. 

vb11:5.1
Pali: Tattha katamo sammākammanto? 

vb11:5.2
Pali: Pāṇātipātā veramaṇī, adinnādānā veramaṇī, kāmesumicchācārā veramaṇī—

vb11:5.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “sammākammanto”. 

vb11:6.1
Pali: Tattha katamo sammāājīvo? 

vb11:6.2
Pali: Idha ariyasāvako micchāājīvaṁ pahāya sammāājīvena jīvikaṁ kappeti—

vb11:6.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “sammāājīvo”. 

vb11:7.1
Pali: Tattha katamo sammāvāyāmo? 

vb11:7.2
Pali: Idha bhikkhu anuppannānaṁ pāpakānaṁ akusalānaṁ dhammānaṁ anuppādāya chandaṁ janeti vāyamati vīriyaṁ ārabhati cittaṁ paggaṇhāti padahati, 

vb11:7.3
Pali: uppannānaṁ pāpakānaṁ akusalānaṁ dhammānaṁ pahānāya chandaṁ janeti vāyamati vīriyaṁ ārabhati cittaṁ paggaṇhāti padahati, 

vb11:7.4
Pali: anuppannānaṁ kusalānaṁ dhammānaṁ uppādāya chandaṁ janeti vāyamati vīriyaṁ ārabhati cittaṁ paggaṇhāti padahati, 

vb11:7.5
Pali: uppannānaṁ kusalānaṁ dhammānaṁ ṭhitiyā asammosāya bhiyyobhāvāya vepullāya bhāvanāya pāripūriyā chandaṁ janeti vāyamati vīriyaṁ ārabhati cittaṁ paggaṇhāti padahati—

vb11:7.6
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “sammāvāyāmo”. 

vb11:8.1
Pali: Tattha katamā sammāsati? 

vb11:8.2
Pali: Idha bhikkhu kāye kāyānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaṁ, 

vb11:8.3
Pali: vedanāsu vedanānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaṁ, 

vb11:8.4
Pali: citte cittānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaṁ, 

vb11:8.5
Pali: dhammesu dhammānupassī viharati ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhādomanassaṁ—

vb11:8.6
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “sammāsati”. 

vb11:9.1
Pali: Tattha katamo sammāsamādhi? 

vb11:9.2
Pali: Idha bhikkhu vivicceva kāmehi vivicca akusalehi dhammehi savitakkaṁ savicāraṁ vivekajaṁ pītisukhaṁ paṭhamaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati; 

vb11:9.3
Pali: vitakkavicārānaṁ vūpasamā ajjhattaṁ sampasādanaṁ cetaso ekodibhāvaṁ avitakkaṁ avicāraṁ samādhijaṁ pītisukhaṁ dutiyaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati; 

vb11:9.4
Pali: pītiyā ca virāgā upekkhako ca viharati sato ca sampajāno sukhañca kāyena paṭisaṁvedeti, yaṁ taṁ ariyā ācikkhanti “upekkhako satimā sukhavihārī”ti tatiyaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati; 

vb11:9.5
Pali: sukhassa ca pahānā dukkhassa ca pahānā pubbeva somanassadomanassānaṁ atthaṅgamā adukkhamasukhaṁ upekkhāsatipārisuddhiṁ catutthaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati—

vb11:9.6
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “sammāsamādhi”.

Pali: Ariyo aṭṭhaṅgiko maggo, seyyathidaṁ—

vb11:10.2

Pali: Tattha katamā sammādiṭṭhi? 

vb11:11.2

vb11:11.3
Pali: sammāsaṅkappaṁ bhāveti …pe… 

vb11:11.4
Pali: sammāvācaṁ bhāveti …pe…

vb11:41.0
Pali: 3. Pañhāpucchaka 

vb11:41.1
Pali: Ariyo aṭṭhaṅgiko maggo, seyyathidaṁ—

vb11:41.2
Pali: sammādiṭṭhi, sammāsaṅkappo, sammāvācā, sammākammanto, sammāājīvo, sammāvāyāmo, sammāsati, sammāsamādhi. 

vb11:42.1
Pali: Aṭṭhannaṁ maggaṅgānaṁ kati kusalā, kati akusalā, kati abyākatā …pe… kati saraṇā, kati araṇā? 

vb11:43.0
Pali: 3.1. Tika 

vb11:43.1
Pali: Siyā kusalā, siyā abyākatā. 

vb11:44.1
Pali: Sammāsaṅkappo sukhāya vedanāya sampayutto; 

vb11:44.2
Pali: satta maggaṅgā siyā sukhāya vedanāya sampayuttā, siyā adukkhamasukhāya vedanāya sampayuttā. 

vb11:45.1
Pali: Siyā vipākā, siyā vipākadhammadhammā. 

vb11:46.1
Pali: Anupādinnaanupādāniyā. 

vb11:47.1
Pali: Asaṅkiliṭṭhaasaṅkilesikā. 

vb11:48.1
Pali: Sammāsaṅkappo avitakkavicāramatto; 

vb11:48.2
Pali: satta maggaṅgā siyā savitakkasavicārā, siyā avitakkavicāramattā, siyā avitakkaavicārā. 

vb11:49.1
Pali: Sammāsaṅkappo pītisahagato, sukhasahagato, na upekkhāsahagato; 

vb11:49.2
Pali: satta maggaṅgā siyā pītisahagatā, siyā sukhasahagatā, siyā upekkhāsahagatā. 

vb11:50.1
Pali: Neva dassanena na bhāvanāya pahātabbā. 

vb11:51.1
Pali: Neva dassanena na bhāvanāya pahātabbahetukā. 

vb11:52.1
Pali: Siyā apacayagāmino, siyā nevācayagāmināpacayagāmino. 

vb11:53.1
Pali: Siyā sekkhā, siyā asekkhā. 

vb11:54.1
Pali: Appamāṇā. 

vb11:55.1
Pali: Appamāṇārammaṇā. 

vb11:56.1
Pali: Paṇītā. 

vb11:57.1
Pali: Siyā sammattaniyatā, siyā aniyatā. 

vb11:58.1
Pali: Na maggārammaṇā, siyā maggahetukā, siyā maggādhipatino; 

vb11:58.2
Pali: siyā na vattabbā “maggahetukā”tipi, “maggādhipatino”tipi. 

vb11:59.1
Pali: Siyā uppannā, siyā anuppannā, siyā uppādino. 

vb11:60.1
Pali: Siyā atītā, siyā anāgatā, siyā paccuppannā. 

vb11:61.1
Pali: Na vattabbā “atītārammaṇā”tipi, “anāgatārammaṇā”tipi, “paccuppannārammaṇā”tipi. 

vb11:62.1
Pali: Siyā ajjhattā, siyā bahiddhā, siyā ajjhattabahiddhā. 

vb11:63.1
Pali: Bahiddhārammaṇā. 

vb11:64.1
Pali: Anidassanaappaṭighā. 

vb11:65.0.1
Pali: 3.2. 3.2 Duka 

vb11:65.0.2
Pali: 3.2.1. Hetugocchaka 

vb11:65.1
Pali: Sammādiṭṭhi hetu, satta maggaṅgā na hetū, sahetukā, hetusampayuttā. 

vb11:65.2
Pali: Sammādiṭṭhi hetu ceva sahetukā ca, satta maggaṅgā na vattabbā “hetū ceva sahetukā cā”ti, sahetukā ceva na ca hetū. 

vb11:65.3
Pali: Sammādiṭṭhi hetu ceva hetusampayuttā ca, satta maggaṅgā na vattabbā “hetū ceva hetusampayuttā cā”ti, hetusampayuttā ceva na ca hetū. 

vb11:65.4
Pali: Satta maggaṅgā na hetū sahetukā, sammādiṭṭhi na vattabbā “na hetu sahetukā”tipi, “na hetu ahetukā”tipi.

Pali segments

vb12:0.1
Pali: Vibhaṅga 

vb12:0.2
Pali: Jhānavibhaṅga 

vb12:1.0
Pali: 1. Suttantabhājanīya 

vb12:1.1
Pali: Idha bhikkhu pātimokkhasaṁvarasaṁvuto viharati, ācāragocarasampanno, aṇumattesu vajjesu bhayadassāvī, samādāya sikkhati sikkhāpadesu indriyesu guttadvāro bhojane mattaññū pubbarattāpararattaṁ jāgariyānuyogamanuyutto sātaccaṁ nepakkaṁ bodhipakkhikānaṁ dhammānaṁ bhāvanānuyogamanuyutto. 

vb12:2.1
Pali: So abhikkante paṭikkante sampajānakārī hoti, ālokite vilokite sampajānakārī hoti, samiñjite pasārite sampajānakārī hoti, saṅghāṭipattacīvaradhāraṇe sampajānakārī hoti, asite pīte khāyite sāyite sampajānakārī hoti, uccārapassāvakamme sampajānakārī hoti, gate ṭhite nisinne sutte jāgarite bhāsite tuṇhībhāve sampajānakārī hoti. 

vb12:3.1
Pali: So vivittaṁ senāsanaṁ bhajati araññaṁ rukkhamūlaṁ pabbataṁ kandaraṁ giriguhaṁ susānaṁ vanapatthaṁ abbhokāsaṁ palālapuñjaṁ appasaddaṁ appanigghosaṁ vijanavātaṁ manussarāhasseyyakaṁ paṭisallānasāruppaṁ. 

vb12:3.2
Pali: So araññagato vā rukkhamūlagato vā suññāgāragato vā nisīdati pallaṅkaṁ ābhujitvā ujuṁ kāyaṁ paṇidhāya parimukhaṁ satiṁ upaṭṭhapetvā. 

vb12:4.1
Pali: So abhijjhaṁ loke pahāya vigatābhijjhena cetasā viharati, abhijjhāya cittaṁ parisodheti. 

vb12:4.2
Pali: Byāpādapadosaṁ pahāya abyāpannacitto viharati sabbapāṇabhūtahitānukampī, byāpādapadosā cittaṁ parisodheti. 

vb12:4.3
Pali: Thinamiddhaṁ pahāya vigatathinamiddho viharati ālokasaññī sato sampajāno, thinamiddhā cittaṁ parisodheti. 

vb12:4.4
Pali: Uddhaccakukkuccaṁ pahāya anuddhato viharati ajjhattaṁ vūpasantacitto, uddhaccakukkuccā cittaṁ parisodheti. 

vb12:4.5
Pali: Vicikicchaṁ pahāya tiṇṇavicikiccho viharati akathaṅkathī kusalesu dhammesu, vicikicchāya cittaṁ parisodheti. 

vb12:5.1
Pali: So ime pañca nīvaraṇe pahāya cetaso upakkilese paññāya dubbalīkaraṇe vivicceva kāmehi vivicca akusalehi dhammehi savitakkaṁ savicāraṁ vivekajaṁ pītisukhaṁ paṭhamaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati; 

vb12:5.2
Pali: vitakkavicārānaṁ vūpasamā ajjhattaṁ sampasādanaṁ cetaso ekodibhāvaṁ avitakkaṁ avicāraṁ samādhijaṁ pītisukhaṁ dutiyaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati; 

vb12:5.3
Pali: pītiyā ca virāgā upekkhako ca viharati sato ca sampajāno sukhañca kāyena paṭisaṁvedeti, yaṁ taṁ ariyā ācikkhanti—“upekkhako satimā sukhavihārī”ti tatiyaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati; 

vb12:5.4
Pali: sukhassa ca pahānā dukkhassa ca pahānā pubbeva somanassadomanassānaṁ atthaṅgamā adukkhamasukhaṁ upekkhāsatipārisuddhiṁ catutthaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati; 

vb12:5.5
Pali: sabbaso rūpasaññānaṁ samatikkamā paṭighasaññānaṁ atthaṅgamā nānattasaññānaṁ amanasikārā “ananto ākāso”ti ākāsānañcāyatanaṁ upasampajja viharati; 

vb12:5.6
Pali: sabbaso ākāsānañcāyatanaṁ samatikkamma “anantaṁ viññāṇan”ti viññāṇañcāyatanaṁ upasampajja viharati; 

vb12:5.7
Pali: sabbaso viññāṇañcāyatanaṁ samatikkamma “natthi kiñcī”ti ākiñcaññāyatanaṁ upasampajja viharati; 

vb12:5.8
Pali: sabbaso ākiñcaññāyatanaṁ samatikkamma nevasaññānāsaññāyatanaṁ upasampajja viharati. 

vb12:6.1
Pali: Mātikā. 

vb12:7.1
Pali: “Idhā”ti imissā diṭṭhiyā, imissā khantiyā, imissā ruciyā, imasmiṁ ādāye, imasmiṁ dhamme, imasmiṁ vinaye, imasmiṁ dhammavinaye, imasmiṁ pāvacane, imasmiṁ brahmacariye, imasmiṁ satthusāsane. 

vb12:7.2
Pali: Tena vuccati “idhā”ti. 

vb12:8.1
Pali: “Bhikkhū”ti samaññāya bhikkhu, paṭiññāya bhikkhu, bhikkhatīti bhikkhu, bhikkhakoti bhikkhu, bhikkhācariyaṁ ajjhupagatoti bhikkhu, bhinnapaṭadharoti bhikkhu, bhindati pāpake akusale dhammeti bhikkhu, bhinnattā pāpakānaṁ akusalānaṁ dhammānaṁ bhikkhu, odhiso kilesānaṁ pahānā bhikkhu, anodhiso kilesānaṁ pahānā bhikkhu, sekkho bhikkhu, asekkho bhikkhu, nevasekkhanāsekkho bhikkhu, aggo bhikkhu, bhadro bhikkhu, maṇḍo bhikkhu, sāro bhikkhu, samaggena saṅghena ñatticatutthena kammena akuppena ṭhānārahena upasampanno bhikkhu. 

vb12:9.1
Pali: “Pātimokkhan”ti sīlaṁ patiṭṭhā ādi caraṇaṁ saṁyamo saṁvaro mokkhaṁ pāmokkhaṁ kusalānaṁ dhammānaṁ samāpattiyā. 

vb12:9.2
Pali: “Saṁvaro”ti kāyiko avītikkamo, vācasiko avītikkamo, kāyikavācasiko avītikkamo. 

vb12:9.3

vb12:9.4

vb12:11.1

vb12:12.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “anācāro”. 

vb12:12.4
Pali: Sabbampi dussīlyaṁ anācāro. 

vb12:12.5

Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “anācāro”. 

vb12:13.1
Pali: Tattha katamo ācāro? 

vb12:13.2

vb12:13.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “ācāro”. 

vb12:13.4

vb12:13.5

vb12:13.6

vb12:14.1
Pali: “Gocaro”ti atthi gocaro, atthi agocaro. 

vb12:15.1

vb12:15.2
Pali: Idhekacco vesiyāgocaro vā hoti vidhavāgocaro vā thullakumārigocaro vā paṇḍakagocaro vā bhikkhunigocaro vā pānāgāragocaro vā, saṁsaṭṭho viharati rājūhi rājamahāmattehi titthiyehi titthiyasāvakehi ananulomikena saṁsaggena; 

vb12:15.3
Pali: yāni vā pana tāni kulāni assaddhāni appasannāni anopānabhūtāni akkosakaparibhāsakāni anatthakāmāni ahitakāmāni aphāsukakāmāni ayogakkhemakāmāni bhikkhūnaṁ bhikkhunīnaṁ upāsakānaṁ upāsikānaṁ, tathārūpāni kulāni sevati bhajati payirupāsati—

vb12:15.4
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “agocaro”. 

vb12:16.1
Pali: Tattha katamo gocaro? 

vb12:16.2

vb12:16.3
Pali: yāni vā pana tāni kulāni saddhāni pasannāni opānabhūtāni kāsāvapajjotāni isivātapaṭivātāni atthakāmāni hitakāmāni phāsukakāmāni yogakkhemakāmāni bhikkhūnaṁ bhikkhunīnaṁ upāsakānaṁ upāsikānaṁ, tathārūpāni kulāni sevati bhajati payirupāsati—

vb12:16.4
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “gocaro”.

vb12:19.1

vb12:22.1

vb12:24.3

vb12:25.1

Pali: “Viññāṇañcāyatanan”ti viññāṇañcāyatanaṁ samāpannassa vā upapannassa vā diṭṭhadhammasukhavihārissa vā cittacetasikā dhammā. 

vb12:157.1
Pali: “Upasampajjā”ti yo viññāṇañcāyatanassa lābho paṭilābho patti sampatti phusanā sacchikiriyā upasampadā. 

vb12:158.1
Pali: “Viharatī”ti …pe… 

vb12:158.2
Pali: tena vuccati “viharatī”ti. 

vb12:159.1
Pali: “Sabbaso viññāṇañcāyatanaṁ samatikkammā”ti imaṁ viññāṇañcāyatanaṁ atikkanto hoti vītikkanto samatikkanto. 

vb12:159.2
Pali: Tena vuccati “sabbaso viññāṇañcāyatanaṁ samatikkammā”ti. 

vb12:160.1
Pali: “Natthi kiñcī”ti taṁyeva viññāṇaṁ bhāveti vibhāveti antaradhāpeti, “natthi kiñcī”ti passati. 

vb12:160.2
Pali: Tena vuccati “natthi kiñcī”ti. 

vb12:161.1
Pali: “Ākiñcaññāyatanan”ti ākiñcaññāyatanaṁ samāpannassa vā upapannassa vā diṭṭhadhammasukhavihārissa vā cittacetasikā dhammā.

vb12:165.1

Pali: Idha bhikkhu yasmiṁ samaye lokuttaraṁ jhānaṁ bhāveti niyyānikaṁ apacayagāmiṁ diṭṭhigatānaṁ pahānāya paṭhamāya bhūmiyā pattiyā vitakkavicārānaṁ vūpasamā …pe… dutiyaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati dukkhapaṭipadaṁ dandhābhiññaṁ, tasmiṁ samaye phasso hoti …pe… avikkhepo hoti. 

vb12:201.3
Pali: Ime dhammā kusalā. 

vb12:201.4
Pali: Tasseva lokuttarassa kusalassa jhānassa katattā bhāvitattā vipākaṁ vitakkavicārānaṁ vūpasamā …pe… dutiyaṁ jhānaṁ …pe… 

vb12:201.5
Pali: tatiyaṁ jhānaṁ …pe… 

vb12:201.6
Pali: catutthaṁ jhānaṁ …pe… 

vb12:201.7
Pali: paṭhamaṁ jhānaṁ …pe… 

vb12:201.8
Pali: pañcamaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati dukkhapaṭipadaṁ dandhābhiññaṁ suññataṁ, tasmiṁ samaye duvaṅgikaṁ jhānaṁ hoti—

vb12:201.9
Pali: upekkhā, cittassekaggatā. 

vb12:201.10
Pali: Idaṁ vuccati “pañcamaṁ jhānaṁ”. 

vb12:201.11
Pali: Avasesā dhammā jhānasampayuttā. 

vb12:202.0
Pali: 2.7. Rūpārūpāvacarakiriya 

vb12:202.1
Pali: Cattāri jhānāni—

vb12:202.2
Pali: paṭhamaṁ jhānaṁ, dutiyaṁ jhānaṁ, tatiyaṁ jhānaṁ, catutthaṁ jhānaṁ. 

vb12:203.1
Pali: Tattha katamaṁ paṭhamaṁ jhānaṁ? 

vb12:203.2
Pali: Idha bhikkhu yasmiṁ samaye rūpāvacaraṁ jhānaṁ bhāveti kiriyaṁ neva kusalaṁ nākusalaṁ na ca kammavipākaṁ diṭṭhadhammasukhavihāraṁ vivicceva kāmehi …pe… paṭhamaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati pathavīkasiṇaṁ, tasmiṁ samaye pañcaṅgikaṁ jhānaṁ hoti—

vb12:203.3
Pali: vitakko, vicāro, pīti, sukhaṁ, cittassekaggatā. 

vb12:203.4
Pali: Idaṁ vuccati “paṭhamaṁ jhānaṁ”. 

vb12:203.5
Pali: Avasesā dhammā jhānasampayuttā. 

vb12:204.1
Pali: Tattha katamaṁ dutiyaṁ jhānaṁ? 

vb12:204.2
Pali: Idha bhikkhu yasmiṁ samaye rūpāvacaraṁ jhānaṁ bhāveti kiriyaṁ neva kusalaṁ nākusalaṁ na ca kammavipākaṁ diṭṭhadhammasukhavihāraṁ vitakkavicārānaṁ vūpasamā …pe… dutiyaṁ jhānaṁ …pe… 

vb12:204.3
Pali: tatiyaṁ jhānaṁ …pe… 

vb12:204.4
Pali: catutthaṁ jhānaṁ …pe… 

vb12:204.5
Pali: paṭhamaṁ jhānaṁ …pe… 

vb12:204.6
Pali: pañcamaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati pathavīkasiṇaṁ, tasmiṁ samaye duvaṅgikaṁ jhānaṁ hoti—

vb12:204.7
Pali: upekkhā, cittassekaggatā. 

vb12:204.8
Pali: Idaṁ vuccati “pañcamaṁ jhānaṁ”. 

vb12:204.9
Pali: Avasesā dhammā jhānasampayuttā. 

vb12:205.1
Pali: Idha bhikkhu yasmiṁ samaye arūpāvacaraṁ jhānaṁ bhāveti kiriyaṁ neva kusalaṁ nākusalaṁ na ca kammavipākaṁ diṭṭhadhammasukhavihāraṁ sabbaso ākiñcaññāyatanaṁ samatikkamma nevasaññānāsaññāyatanasaññāsahagataṁ sukhassa ca pahānā …pe… catutthaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati, tasmiṁ samaye duvaṅgikaṁ jhānaṁ hoti—

vb12:205.2
Pali: upekkhā, cittassekaggatā. 

vb12:205.3
Pali: Idaṁ vuccati “catutthaṁ jhānaṁ”. 

vb12:205.4
Pali: Avasesā dhammā jhānasampayuttāti. 

vb12:206.1
Pali: Abhidhammabhājanīyaṁ. 

vb12:207.0
Pali: 3. Pañhāpucchaka 

vb12:207.1
Pali: Cattāri jhānāni—

vb12:207.2
Pali: idha bhikkhu vivicceva kāmehi vivicca akusalehi dhammehi savitakkaṁ savicāraṁ vivekajaṁ pītisukhaṁ paṭhamaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati …pe… 

vb12:207.3
Pali: vitakkavicārānaṁ vūpasamā ajjhattaṁ sampasādanaṁ cetaso ekodibhāvaṁ avitakkaṁ avicāraṁ samādhijaṁ pītisukhaṁ dutiyaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati …pe… 

vb12:207.4
Pali: pītiyā ca virāgā upekkhako ca viharati sato ca sampajāno sukhañca kāyena paṭisaṁvedeti, yaṁ taṁ ariyā ācikkhanti—“upekkhako satimā sukhavihārī”ti tatiyaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati …pe… 

vb12:207.5
Pali: sukhassa ca pahānā dukkhassa ca pahānā pubbeva somanassadomanassānaṁ atthaṅgamā adukkhamasukhaṁ upekkhāsatipārisuddhiṁ catutthaṁ jhānaṁ upasampajja viharati. 

vb12:208.1
Pali: Catunnaṁ jhānānaṁ kati kusalā, kati akusalā, kati abyākatā …pe… kati saraṇā, kati araṇā? 

vb12:209.0
Pali: 3.1. Tika 

vb12:209.1
Pali: Siyā kusalā, siyā abyākatā. 

vb12:210.1
Pali: Tīṇi jhānāni—

vb12:210.2
Pali: etthuppannaṁ sukhaṁ vedanaṁ ṭhapetvā sukhāya vedanāya sampayuttā, catutthaṁ jhānaṁ—

vb12:210.3
Pali: etthuppannaṁ adukkhamasukhaṁ vedanaṁ ṭhapetvā adukkhamasukhāya vedanāya sampayuttaṁ. 

vb12:211.1
Pali: Siyā vipākā, siyā vipākadhammadhammā, siyā nevavipākanavipākadhammadhammā. 

vb12:212.1
Pali: Siyā upādinnupādāniyā, siyā anupādinnupādāniyā, siyā anupādinnaanupādāniyā. 

vb12:213.1
Pali: Siyā asaṅkiliṭṭhasaṅkilesikā, siyā asaṅkiliṭṭhaasaṅkilesikā. 

vb12:214.1
Pali: Paṭhamaṁ jhānaṁ—

vb12:214.2
Pali: etthuppanne vitakkavicāre ṭhapetvā savitakkaṁ savicāraṁ, tīṇi jhānāni avitakkaavicārā. 

vb12:215.1
Pali: Dve jhānāni—

vb12:215.2
Pali: etthuppannaṁ pītiṁ ṭhapetvā pītisahagatā, tīṇi jhānāni—

vb12:215.3
Pali: etthuppannaṁ sukhaṁ ṭhapetvā sukhasahagatā, catutthaṁ jhānaṁ—

vb12:215.4
Pali: etthuppannaṁ upekkhaṁ ṭhapetvā upekkhāsahagataṁ. 

vb12:216.1
Pali: Neva dassanena na bhāvanāya pahātabbā. 

vb12:217.1
Pali: Neva dassanena na bhāvanāya pahātabbahetukā. 

vb12:218.1
Pali: Siyā ācayagāmino, siyā apacayagāmino, siyā nevācayagāmināpacayagāmino. 

vb12:219.1
Pali: Siyā sekkhā, siyā asekkhā, siyā nevasekkhanāsekkhā. 

vb12:220.1
Pali: Siyā mahaggatā, siyā appamāṇā. 

vb12:221.1
Pali: Tīṇi jhānāni na vattabbā “parittārammaṇā”tipi, “mahaggatārammaṇā”tipi, siyā appamāṇārammaṇā, siyā na vattabbā “appamāṇārammaṇā”ti; 

vb12:221.2
Pali: catutthaṁ jhānaṁ siyā parittārammaṇaṁ, siyā mahaggatārammaṇaṁ, siyā appamāṇārammaṇaṁ; 

vb12:221.3
Pali: siyā na vattabbaṁ “parittārammaṇan”tipi, “mahaggatārammaṇan”tipi, “appamāṇārammaṇan”tipi. 

vb12:222.1
Pali: Siyā majjhimā, siyā paṇītā. 

vb12:223.1
Pali: Siyā sammattaniyatā, siyā aniyatā. 

vb12:224.1
Pali: Tīṇi jhānāni na maggārammaṇā, siyā maggahetukā, siyā maggādhipatino, siyā na vattabbā “maggahetukā”tipi, “maggādhipatino”tipi; 

vb12:224.2
Pali: catutthaṁ jhānaṁ siyā maggārammaṇaṁ, siyā maggahetukaṁ, siyā maggādhipati, siyā na vattabbaṁ “maggārammaṇan”tipi, “maggahetukan”tipi “maggādhipatī”tipi. 

vb12:225.1
Pali: Siyā uppannā, siyā anuppannā, siyā uppādino. 

vb12:226.1
Pali: Siyā atītā, siyā anāgatā, siyā paccuppannā. 

vb12:227.1
Pali: Tīṇi jhānāni na vattabbā “atītārammaṇā”tipi, “anāgatārammaṇā”tipi, “paccuppannārammaṇā”tipi; 

vb12:227.2
Pali: catutthaṁ jhānaṁ siyā atītārammaṇaṁ, siyā anāgatārammaṇaṁ, siyā paccuppannārammaṇaṁ, siyā na vattabbaṁ “atītārammaṇan”tipi, “anāgatārammaṇan”tipi, “paccuppannārammaṇan”tipi. 

vb12:228.1
Pali: Siyā ajjhattā, siyā bahiddhā, siyā ajjhattabahiddhā. 

vb12:229.1
Pali: Tīṇi jhānāni bahiddhārammaṇā, catutthaṁ jhānaṁ siyā ajjhattārammaṇaṁ, siyā bahiddhārammaṇaṁ, siyā ajjhattabahiddhārammaṇaṁ, siyā na vattabbaṁ “ajjhattārammaṇan”tipi, “bahiddhārammaṇan”tipi, “ajjhattabahiddhārammaṇan”tipi. 

vb12:230.1
Pali: Anidassanaappaṭighā. 

vb12:231.0
Pali: 3.2. Duka 

vb12:231.1
Pali: Na hetū, sahetukā, hetusampayuttā, na vattabbā “hetū ceva sahetukā cā”ti, sahetukā ceva na ca hetū, na vattabbā “hetū ceva hetusampayuttā cā”ti, hetusampayuttā ceva na ca hetū, na hetū sahetukā. 

vb12:232.1
Pali: Sappaccayā, saṅkhatā, anidassanā, appaṭighā, arūpā, siyā lokiyā, siyā lokuttarā, kenaci viññeyyā, kenaci na viññeyyā. 

vb12:233.1
Pali: No āsavā, siyā sāsavā, siyā anāsavā, āsavavippayuttā, na vattabbā “āsavā ceva sāsavā cā”ti, siyā sāsavā ceva no ca āsavā, siyā na vattabbā “sāsavā ceva no ca āsavā”ti. 

vb12:233.2
Pali: Na vattabbā “āsavā ceva āsavasampayuttā cā”tipi, “āsavasampayuttā ceva no ca āsavā”tipi. 

vb12:233.3
Pali: Siyā āsavavippayuttā sāsavā, siyā āsavavippayuttā anāsavā.

Pali: No saṁyojanā …pe…

vb12:234.6

vb12:234.7
Pali: sārammaṇā, no cittā, cetasikā, cittasampayuttā, cittasaṁsaṭṭhā, cittasamuṭṭhānā, cittasahabhuno, cittānuparivattino, cittasaṁsaṭṭhasamuṭṭhānā, cittasaṁsaṭṭhasamuṭṭhānasahabhuno, cittasaṁsaṭṭhasamuṭṭhānānuparivattino, bāhirā, no upādā, siyā upādinnā, siyā anupādinnā. 

vb12:235.1
Pali: No upādānā …pe… 

vb12:235.2
Pali: no kilesā …pe… 

vb12:235.3
Pali: na dassanena pahātabbā, na bhāvanāya pahātabbā, na dassanena pahātabbahetukā, na bhāvanāya pahātabbahetukā. 

vb12:235.4

vb12:235.5

vb12:235.7

vb12:235.8
Pali: Dve jhānāni—

vb12:235.9

vb12:235.10
Pali: Dve jhānāni—

vb12:235.13

vb12:235.14
Pali: Catutthaṁ jhānaṁ—

vb12:235.15
Pali: etthuppannaṁ upekkhaṁ ṭhapetvā upekkhāsahagataṁ, tīṇi jhānāni upekkhāsahagatā, na kāmāvacarā, siyā rūpāvacarā, siyā na rūpāvacarā, tīṇi jhānāni na arūpāvacarā, catutthaṁ jhānaṁ siyā arūpāvacaraṁ, siyā na arūpāvacaraṁ, siyā pariyāpannā, siyā apariyāpannā, siyā niyyānikā, siyā aniyyānikā, siyā niyatā, siyā aniyatā, siyā sauttarā, siyā anuttarā, araṇāti. 

vb12:236.1
Pali: Pañhāpucchakaṁ. 

vb12:237.1
Pali: Jhānavibhaṅgo niṭṭhito.

vb13:0.1
Pali: Vibhaṅga 

vb13:0.2
Pali: Appamaññāvibhaṅga 

vb13:1.0
Pali: 1. Suttantabhājanīya 

vb13:1.1
Pali: Catasso appamaññāyo—

vb13:1.2
Pali: idha bhikkhu mettāsahagatena cetasā ekaṁ disaṁ pharitvā viharati, tathā dutiyaṁ, tathā tatiyaṁ, tathā catutthaṁ. 

vb13:1.3
Pali: Iti uddhamadho tiriyaṁ sabbadhi sabbattatāya sabbāvantaṁ lokaṁ mettāsahagatena cetasā vipulena mahaggatena appamāṇena averena abyāpajjena pharitvā viharati. 

vb13:1.4
Pali: Karuṇāsahagatena cetasā ekaṁ disaṁ pharitvā viharati, tathā dutiyaṁ, tathā tatiyaṁ, tathā catutthaṁ. 

vb13:1.5
Pali: Iti uddhamadho tiriyaṁ sabbadhi sabbattatāya sabbāvantaṁ lokaṁ karuṇāsahagatena cetasā vipulena mahaggatena appamāṇena averena abyāpajjena pharitvā viharati. 

vb13:1.6
Pali: Muditāsahagatena cetasā ekaṁ disaṁ pharitvā viharati, tathā dutiyaṁ, tathā tatiyaṁ, tathā catutthaṁ. 

vb13:1.7
Pali: Iti uddhamadho tiriyaṁ sabbadhi sabbattatāya sabbāvantaṁ lokaṁ muditāsahagatena cetasā vipulena mahaggatena appamāṇena averena abyāpajjena pharitvā viharati. 

vb13:1.8
Pali: Upekkhāsahagatena cetasā ekaṁ disaṁ pharitvā viharati, tathā dutiyaṁ, tathā tatiyaṁ, tathā catutthaṁ. 

vb13:1.9
Pali: Iti uddhamadho tiriyaṁ sabbadhi sabbattatāya sabbāvantaṁ lokaṁ upekkhāsahagatena cetasā vipulena mahaggatena appamāṇena averena abyāpajjena pharitvā viharati. 

vb13:2.0
Pali: 1.1. Mettā 

vb13:2.1
Pali: Kathañca bhikkhu mettāsahagatena cetasā ekaṁ disaṁ pharitvā viharati? 

vb13:2.2
Pali: Seyyathāpi nāma ekaṁ puggalaṁ piyaṁ manāpaṁ disvā mettāyeyya; 

vb13:2.3
Pali: evameva sabbe satte mettāya pharati. 

vb13:3.1
Pali: Tattha katamā mettā? 

vb13:3.2
Pali: Yā sattesu metti mettāyanā mettāyitattaṁ mettācetovimutti—

vb13:3.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “mettā”. 

vb13:4.1
Pali: Tattha katamaṁ cittaṁ? 

vb13:4.2
Pali: Yaṁ cittaṁ mano mānasaṁ hadayaṁ paṇḍaraṁ mano manāyatanaṁ manindriyaṁ viññāṇaṁ viññāṇakkhandho tajjāmanoviññāṇadhātu—

vb13:4.3
Pali: idaṁ vuccati “cittaṁ”. 

vb13:4.4
Pali: Idaṁ cittaṁ imāya mettāya sahagataṁ hoti sahajātaṁ saṁsaṭṭhaṁ sampayuttaṁ. 

vb13:4.5
Pali: Tena vuccati “mettāsahagatena cetasā”ti. 

vb13:5.1
Pali: “Ekaṁ disan”ti puratthimaṁ vā disaṁ pacchimaṁ vā disaṁ uttaraṁ vā disaṁ dakkhiṇaṁ vā disaṁ uddhaṁ vā adho vā tiriyaṁ vā vidisaṁ vā. 

vb13:6.1
Pali: “Pharitvā”ti pharitvā adhimuccitvā. 

vb13:7.1
Pali: “Viharatī”ti iriyati vattati pāleti yapeti yāpeti carati viharati. 

vb13:7.2
Pali: Tena vuccati “viharatī”ti. 

vb13:8.1
Pali: “Tathā dutiyan”ti yatheva ekaṁ disaṁ tathā dutiyaṁ disaṁ tathā tatiyaṁ disaṁ tathā catutthaṁ disaṁ tathā uddhaṁ tathā adho tathā tiriyaṁ tathā vidisaṁ. 

vb13:9.1
Pali: “Sabbadhi sabbattatāya sabbāvantaṁ lokan”ti sabbena sabbaṁ sabbathā sabbaṁ asesaṁ nissesaṁ. 

vb13:9.2
Pali: Pariyādāyavacanametaṁ—

vb13:9.3
Pali: “sabbadhi sabbattatāya sabbāvantaṁ lokan”ti. 

vb13:10.1
Pali: “Mettāsahagatena cetasā”ti tattha katamā mettā? 

vb13:10.2
Pali: Yā sattesu metti mettāyanā mettāyitattaṁ mettācetovimutti—

vb13:10.3
Pali: ayaṁ vuccati “mettā”. 

vb13:11.1
Pali: Tattha katamaṁ cittaṁ? 

vb13:11.2

vb13:11.3
Pali: idaṁ vuccati “cittaṁ”. 

vb13:11.4
Pali: Idaṁ cittaṁ imāya mettāya sahagataṁ hoti sahajātaṁ saṁsaṭṭhaṁ sampayuttaṁ. 

vb13:11.5
Pali: Tena vuccati “mettāsahagatena cetasā”ti. 

vb13:12.1
Pali: “Vipulenā”ti yaṁ vipulaṁ taṁ mahaggataṁ, yaṁ mahaggataṁ taṁ appamāṇaṁ, yaṁ appamāṇaṁ so avero, yo avero so abyāpajjo. 

vb13:13.1
Pali: “Pharitvā”ti pharitvā adhimuccitvā. 

vb13:14.1
Pali: “Viharatī”ti …pe… 

vb13:14.2

vb13:15.0

vb13:15.1

vb13:15.2

vb13:18.1
Pali: “Ekaṁ disan”ti puratthimaṁ vā disaṁ pacchimaṁ vā disaṁ uttaraṁ vā disaṁ dakkhiṇaṁ vā disaṁ uddhaṁ vā adho vā tiriyaṁ vā vidisaṁ vā.

vb13:91.0
Pali: 3. Pañhāpucchaka 

vb13:91.1
Pali: Catasso appamaññāyo—

vb13:92.1
Pali: Idha bhikkhu mettāsahagatena cetasā ekaṁ disaṁ pharitvā viharati tathā dutiyaṁ tathā tatiyaṁ tathā catutthaṁ, iti uddhamadho tiriyaṁ sabbadhi sabbattatāya sabbāvantaṁ lokaṁ mettāsahagatena cetasā vipulena mahaggatena appamāṇena averena abyāpajjena pharitvā viharati. 

vb13:93.1
Pali: Karuṇāsahagatena cetasā ekaṁ disaṁ pharitvā viharati tathā dutiyaṁ tathā tatiyaṁ tathā catutthaṁ, iti uddhamadho tiriyaṁ sabbadhi sabbattatāya sabbāvantaṁ lokaṁ karuṇāsahagatena cetasā vipulena mahaggatena appamāṇena averena abyāpajjena pharitvā viharati. 

vb13:94.1
Pali: Muditāsahagatena cetasā ekaṁ disaṁ pharitvā viharati tathā dutiyaṁ tathā tatiyaṁ tathā catutthaṁ, iti uddhamadho tiriyaṁ sabbadhi sabbattatāya sabbāvantaṁ lokaṁ muditāsahagatena cetasā vipulena mahaggatena appamāṇena averena abyāpajjena pharitvā viharati. 

vb13:95.1
Pali: Upekkhāsahagatena cetasā ekaṁ disaṁ pharitvā viharati tathā dutiyaṁ tathā tatiyaṁ tathā catutthaṁ, iti uddhamadho tiriyaṁ sabbadhi sabbattatāya sabbāvantaṁ lokaṁ upekkhāsahagatena cetasā vipulena mahaggatena appamāṇena averena abyāpajjena pharitvā viharati. 

vb13:96.1
Pali: Catunnaṁ appamaññānaṁ kati kusalā, kati akusalā, kati abyākatā …pe… kati saraṇā, kati araṇā? 

vb13:97.0
Pali: 3.1. Tika 

vb13:97.1
Pali: Siyā kusalā, siyā abyākatā. 

vb13:98.1
Pali: Tisso appamaññāyo sukhāya vedanāya sampayuttā, upekkhā adukkhamasukhāya vedanāya sampayuttā. 

vb13:99.1
Pali: Siyā vipākā, siyā vipākadhammadhammā, siyā nevavipākanavipākadhammadhammā. 

vb13:100.1
Pali: Siyā upādinnupādāniyā, siyā anupādinnupādāniyā. 

vb13:101.1
Pali: Asaṅkiliṭṭhasaṅkilesikā. 

vb13:102.1
Pali: Tisso appamaññāyo siyā savitakkasavicārā, siyā avitakkavicāramattā, siyā avitakkaavicārā; 

vb13:102.2
Pali: upekkhā avitakkaavicārā. 

vb13:103.1
Pali: Tisso appamaññāyo siyā pītisahagatā, siyā sukhasahagatā, na upekkhāsahagatā, siyā na vattabbā pītisahagatāti; 

vb13:103.2
Pali: upekkhā upekkhāsahagatā. 

vb13:104.1
Pali: Neva dassanena na bhāvanāya pahātabbā. 

vb13:105.1
Pali: Neva dassanena na bhāvanāya pahātabbahetukā. 

vb13:106.1
Pali: Siyā ācayagāmino, siyā nevācayagāmināpacayagāmino. 

vb13:107.1
Pali: Nevasekkhanāsekkhā. 

vb13:108.1
Pali: Mahaggatā. 

vb13:109.1
Pali: Na vattabbā “parittārammaṇā”tipi, “mahaggatārammaṇā”tipi, “appamāṇārammaṇā”tipi. 

vb13:110.1
Pali: Majjhimā. 

vb13:111.1
Pali: Aniyatā. 

vb13:112.1
Pali: Na vattabbā “maggārammaṇā”tipi, “maggahetukā”tipi, “maggādhipatino”tipi. 

vb13:113.1
Pali: Siyā uppannā, siyā anuppannā, siyā uppādino. 

vb13:114.1
Pali: Siyā atītā, siyā anāgatā, siyā paccuppannā. 

vb13:115.1
Pali: Na vattabbā “atītārammaṇā”tipi, “anāgatārammaṇā”tipi, “paccuppannārammaṇā”tipi. 

vb13:116.1
Pali: Siyā ajjhattā, siyā bahiddhā, siyā ajjhattabahiddhā. 

vb13:117.1
Pali: Bahiddhārammaṇā. 

vb13:118.1
Pali: Anidassanaappaṭighā. 

vb13:119.0.1
Pali: 3.2. 3.2 Duka 

vb13:119.0.2
Pali: 3.2.1. Hetugocchaka 

vb13:119.1
Pali: Mettā hetu, tisso appamaññāyo na hetū, sahetukā, hetusampayuttā. 

vb13:119.2
Pali: Mettā hetu ceva sahetukā ca; 

vb13:119.3
Pali: tisso appamaññāyo na vattabbā “hetū ceva sahetukā cā”ti, sahetukā ceva na ca hetū. 

vb13:119.4
Pali: Mettā hetu ceva hetusampayuttā ca; 

vb13:119.5
Pali: tisso appamaññāyo na vattabbā “hetū ceva hetusampayuttā cā”ti, hetusampayuttā ceva na ca hetū. 

vb13:119.6
Pali: Tisso appamaññāyo na hetū sahetukā; 

vb13:119.7
Pali: mettā na vattabbā “na hetu sahetukā”tipi, “na hetu ahetukā”tipi. 

vb13:120.0
Pali: 3.2.2. Cūḷantaraduka 

vb13:120.1
Pali: Sappaccayā, saṅkhatā, anidassanā, appaṭighā, arūpā, lokiyā, kenaci viññeyyā, kenaci na viññeyyā. 

vb13:121.0
Pali: 3.2.3. Āsavagocchaka 

vb13:121.1
Pali: No āsavā, sāsavā, āsavavippayuttā, na vattabbā “āsavā ceva sāsavā cā”ti, sāsavā ceva no ca āsavā, na vattabbā āsavā ceva “āsavasampayuttā cā”tipi, “āsavasampayuttā ceva no ca āsavā”tipi. 

vb13:121.2
Pali: Āsavavippayuttā sāsavā.

vb13:122.6
Pali: no parāmāsā …pe…. 

vb13:123.0

vb13:123.1
Pali: Sārammaṇā, no cittā, cetasikā, cittasampayuttā, cittasaṁsaṭṭhā, cittasamuṭṭhānā, cittasahabhuno, cittānuparivattino, cittasaṁsaṭṭhasamuṭṭhānā, cittasaṁsaṭṭhasamuṭṭhānasahabhuno, cittasaṁsaṭṭhasamuṭṭhānānuparivattino, bāhirā, no upādā, siyā upādinnā, siyā anupādinnā.

vb14:1.0
Pali: 1. Abhidhammabhājanīya 

vb14:1.1
Pali: Pañca sikkhāpadāni—

vb14:1.2
Pali: pāṇātipātā veramaṇī sikkhāpadaṁ, adinnādānā veramaṇī sikkhāpadaṁ, kāmesumicchācārā veramaṇī sikkhāpadaṁ, musāvādā veramaṇī sikkhāpadaṁ, surāmerayamajjapamādaṭṭhānā veramaṇī sikkhāpadaṁ. 

vb14:2.1
Pali: Tattha katamaṁ pāṇātipātā veramaṇī sikkhāpadaṁ? 

vb14:2.2
Pali: Yasmiṁ samaye kāmāvacaraṁ kusalaṁ cittaṁ uppannaṁ hoti somanassasahagataṁ ñāṇasampayuttaṁ pāṇātipātā viramantassa, yā tasmiṁ samaye pāṇātipātā ārati virati paṭivirati veramaṇī akiriyā akaraṇaṁ anajjhāpatti velāanatikkamo setughāto—

vb14:2.3
Pali: idaṁ vuccati “pāṇātipātā veramaṇī sikkhāpadaṁ”. 

vb14:2.4
Pali: Avasesā dhammā veramaṇiyā sampayuttā. 

vb14:3.1
Pali: Tattha katamaṁ pāṇātipātā veramaṇī sikkhāpadaṁ? 

vb14:3.2
Pali: Yasmiṁ samaye kāmāvacaraṁ kusalaṁ cittaṁ uppannaṁ hoti somanassasahagataṁ ñāṇasampayuttaṁ pāṇātipātā viramantassa, yā tasmiṁ samaye cetanā sañcetanā sañcetayitattaṁ—

vb14:3.3
Pali: idaṁ vuccati “pāṇātipātā veramaṇī sikkhāpadaṁ”. 

vb14:3.4
Pali: Avasesā dhammā cetanāya sampayuttā.

vb14:4.3
Pali: idaṁ vuccati “pāṇātipātā veramaṇī sikkhāpadaṁ”.

Pali: Tattha katamaṁ pāṇātipātā veramaṇī sikkhāpadaṁ?

vb14:5.3

vb14:5.9

vb14:6.1

vb14:25.0
Pali: 2. Pañhāpucchaka 

vb14:25.1
Pali: Pañca sikkhāpadāni—

vb14:25.2
Pali: pāṇātipātā veramaṇī sikkhāpadaṁ, adinnādānā veramaṇī sikkhāpadaṁ, kāmesumicchācārā veramaṇī sikkhāpadaṁ, musāvādā veramaṇī sikkhāpadaṁ, surāmerayamajjapamādaṭṭhānā veramaṇī sikkhāpadaṁ. 

vb14:26.1
Pali: Pañcannaṁ sikkhāpadānaṁ kati kusalā, kati akusalā, kati abyākatā …pe… kati saraṇā, kati araṇā? 

vb14:27.0
Pali: 2.1. Tika 

vb14:27.1
Pali: Kusalāyeva. 

vb14:28.1
Pali: Siyā sukhāya vedanāya sampayuttā, siyā adukkhamasukhāya vedanāya sampayuttā. 

vb14:29.1
Pali: Vipākadhammadhammā. 

vb14:30.1
Pali: Anupādinnupādāniyā. 

vb14:31.1
Pali: Asaṅkiliṭṭhasaṅkilesikā. 

vb14:32.1
Pali: Savitakkasavicārā. 

vb14:33.1
Pali: Siyā pītisahagatā, siyā sukhasahagatā, siyā upekkhāsahagatā. 

vb14:34.1
Pali: Neva dassanena na bhāvanāya pahātabbā. 

vb14:35.1
Pali: Neva dassanena na bhāvanāya pahātabbahetukā. 

vb14:36.1
Pali: Ācayagāmino. 

vb14:37.1
Pali: Nevasekkhanāsekkhā. 

vb14:38.1
Pali: Parittā. 

vb14:39.1
Pali: Parittārammaṇā. 

vb14:40.1
Pali: Majjhimā. 

vb14:41.1
Pali: Aniyatā. 

vb14:42.1
Pali: Na vattabbā maggārammaṇātipi, maggahetukātipi, maggādhipatinotipi. 

vb14:43.1
Pali: Siyā uppannā, siyā anuppannā, na vattabbā uppādinoti. 

vb14:44.1
Pali: Siyā atītā, siyā anāgatā, siyā paccuppannā. 

vb14:45.1
Pali: Paccuppannārammaṇā. 

vb14:46.1
Pali: Siyā ajjhattā, siyā bahiddhā, siyā ajjhattabahiddhā. 

vb14:47.1
Pali: Bahiddhārammaṇā. 

vb14:48.1
Pali: Anidassanaappaṭighā. 

vb14:49.0.1
Pali: 2.2. 2.2 Duka 

vb14:49.0.2
Pali: 2.2.1. Hetugocchaka 

vb14:49.1
Pali: Na hetū sahetukā, hetusampayuttā. 

vb14:49.2
Pali: Na vattabbā “hetū ceva sahetukā cā”ti, sahetukā ceva na ca hetū, na vattabbā “hetū ceva hetusampayuttā cā”ti, hetusampayuttā ceva na ca hetū, na hetusahetukā. 

vb14:50.0
Pali: 2.2.2. Cūḷantaraduka 

vb14:50.1
Pali: Sappaccayā, saṅkhatā, anidassanā, appaṭighā, arūpā, lokiyā, kenaci viññeyyā, kenaci na viññeyyā. 

vb14:51.0
Pali: 2.2.3. Āsavagocchaka 

vb14:51.1
Pali: No āsavā, sāsavā, āsavavippayuttā, na vattabbā “āsavā ceva sāsavā cā”ti, sāsavā ceva no ca āsavā, na vattabbā “āsavā ceva āsavasampayuttā cā”tipi, “āsavasampayuttā ceva no ca āsavā”tipi. 

vb14:51.2
Pali: Āsavavippayuttā sāsavā. 

vb14:52.0

vb15:1.2
Pali: atthapaṭisambhidā, dhammapaṭisambhidā, niruttipaṭisambhidā, paṭibhānapaṭisambhidā. 

vb15:1.3
Pali: Atthe ñāṇaṁ atthapaṭisambhidā, dhamme ñāṇaṁ dhammapaṭisambhidā, tatra dhammaniruttābhilāpe ñāṇaṁ niruttipaṭisambhidā, ñāṇesu ñāṇaṁ paṭibhānapaṭisambhidā.

vb15:51.11

vb15:51.12

vb15:51.13
Pali: Ime dhammā abyākatā. 

vb15:51.14
Pali: Imesu dhammesu ñāṇaṁ atthapaṭisambhidā. 

vb15:51.15
Pali: Yāya niruttiyā tesaṁ dhammānaṁ paññatti hoti tatra dhammaniruttābhilāpe ñāṇaṁ niruttipaṭisambhidā. 

vb15:51.16
Pali: Yena ñāṇena tāni ñāṇāni jānāti—

vb15:51.17
Pali: “imāni ñāṇāni idamatthajotakānī”ti, ñāṇesu ñāṇaṁ paṭibhānapaṭisambhidā. 

vb15:52.1

vb15:52.2
Pali: atthapaṭisambhidā, dhammapaṭisambhidā, niruttipaṭisambhidā, paṭibhānapaṭisambhidā. 

vb15:52.3
Pali: Tisso paṭisambhidā kāmāvacarakusalato catūsu ñāṇasampayuttesu cittuppādesu, kiriyato catūsu ñāṇasampayuttesu cittuppādesu uppajjanti. 

vb15:52.4

Pali: Ekavidhena ñāṇavatthu—

vb16:1.2
Pali: pañca viññāṇā na hetū, ahetukā, hetuvippayuttā, sappaccayā, saṅkhatā, arūpā, lokiyā, sāsavā, saṁyojaniyā, ganthaniyā, oghaniyā, yoganiyā, nīvaraṇiyā, parāmaṭṭhā, upādāniyā, saṅkilesikā, abyākatā, sārammaṇā, acetasikā, vipākā, upādinnupādāniyā, asaṅkiliṭṭhasaṅkilesikā, na savitakkasavicārā, na avitakkavicāramattā, avitakkaavicārā, na pītisahagatā, neva dassanena na bhāvanāya pahātabbā, neva dassanena na bhāvanāya pahātabbahetukā, nevācayagāmināpacayagāmino, nevasekkhanāsekkhā, parittā, kāmāvacarā, na rūpāvacarā, na arūpāvacarā, pariyāpannā, no apariyāpannā, aniyatā, aniyyānikā.
